Summoning International Silver Price Conference

British Chancellor Believes It Is Unnecessary

Cotton Industry Groups Express Opinions

▲ Havas News Agency, London, 18th dispatch: Yesterday, British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain declared in the House of Commons that the British government does not intend to convene an international silver price conference in the short term. All sectors of British society attach great importance to the issue of silver price recovery, and there was some surprise upon hearing the news. The organ of the Manchester Guidance Newspaper Cotton Industry Group stated that Lancashire industrialists regretted learning of the government's decision. For six years, the price of silver has risen more than the pound sterling, and British trade with China therefore has the hope of restoring to its former state. It is a pity that the price of silver fluctuates greatly, reaching as much as three and a half pence last Saturday. With this, hoping for economic recovery is inevitable, which is difficult to achieve. Previously, the International Chamber of Commerce organized a committee to study the silver price issue. Recently, the committee submitted a report advocating stabilizing the silver price, stating that an agreement should be concluded between the silver factory owners in the United States and Mexico and the Indian government, which sells a lot of silver. Silver factory owners and sellers can consult automatically without the intervention of the British government, but from our point of view, the British government has no reason not to propose consultation. The reason is that there is no theory of adopting bi-metalism, and the proposal to restore the silver price before the war is not a problem. The current urgent task is only to stabilize the price of silver. In the opinion of the Lancashire industrial community, the importance of this move is only second to the stability of the price of the pound sterling and is unmatched by other matters. The newspaper hopes that the representatives of the Lancashire industrial community will continue to resolutely request the National Cabinet in order to obtain satisfactory results.

Narcotics Trafficking Case Opens Trial

▲ Havas News Agency, 19th dispatch, Basel, Switzerland: The international heroin smuggling case is now on trial. This morning, the court spent a

(10)

Significant amount of time inquiring about a Greek man with mysterious whereabouts. This man is called Ance Sobro and instructed a doctor named Hansche to carry out various activities. The court must investigate this. This Greek man is still a mysterious figure. The court then investigated the case of private trafficking of 716 kilograms of heroin, which Dr. Hansche sold to strangers, and the buyers did not carry licenses to sell narcotics. Dr. Hansche firmly denied selling heroin, saying that he only sold some morphine, which is not prohibited by law, but one package of this drug was chemically tested by customs and confirmed to be heroin rather than morphine. Dr. Hansche said that the customs chemical test was wrong and that he did not receive heroin at Müller's home. What he took at the time were drugs that were not subject to inspection. The experts said that Dr. Hansche's laboratory in Geneva was very simple and could not manufacture large-scale chemical products. There must be another wholesaler in contact with him. Just as the court was about to adjourn, a strange thing happened. A well-known merchant in Basel has been paying attention to this case in the newspapers every day. On this day, he suddenly reported to the court that he had been in constant contact with Anstad Sobro Company in Patras City for several years, so he was willing to provide the court with all necessary information. However, according to the report of the Patras City Police in Greece, no one named Anstad Sobro was found there. The words of the Basel merchant are also very strange.

Important News

The Japanese Army's Invasion of Heilongjiang Province

Beijing Correspondence: Although the Japanese army claims not to invade northern Manchuria after occupying Liaoning and Jilin, their ambitions are actually very strong. They must encompass the three provinces before they will be satisfied. Previously, they instigated Zhang Haipeng, the Garrison Commander of Taoliao, to invade Jiang Province. This is solid proof of their intention to invade northern Manchuria. The Japanese are using Zhang Haipeng to seize power in Jiang Province, intending to divide the entire Northeast, to achieve their so-called "Manchuria-Korea as One" plan. Zhang Haipeng was initially blinded by profit and willing to be used by the Japanese. On October 15th, he advanced his troops to Tailai. The Jiang Province authorities, in order to avoid the scourge of war, not only dispatched considerable forces to defend along the Nenjiang River, and dismantled several spans of the Harge Jiang Bridge to prevent Zhang from advancing, but also sent representatives to meet with Zhang, explaining the greater meaning of the situation. Zhang, also aware of internal divisions and the bombing of his key personnel (his commander, Mr. Xu), and the unreliability of the Japanese, slightly awakened. He withdrew his troops stationed in Tailai back to Taonan. The Japanese, seeing this, became very angry and immediately detained Zhang's family members in Taonan, forcing Zhang to actively advance his troops and seize Jiang Province. On the other hand, using the pretext of repairing the Jiang Bridge, they actually implemented troop advancement on November 3rd. The details of the Japanese army's advancement are recorded day by day as follows: On October 28th, the Nenjiang Harge Jiang Bridge was damaged in several spans to prevent Zhang and others from advancing north. The Japanese Consul in Jiang Province, Mr. Shimizu, notified the Jiang Province authorities on this day, stating that the Tao'an Railway had a loan relationship with the South Manchuria Railway, and the dismantled Jiang Bridge should be repaired by the South Manchuria Railway Company. The Jiang Province Standing Committee immediately rejected the Japanese's unreasonable request, stating that the Japanese request was unreasonable.

On November 2nd, at 10 a.m., Japanese Consul Shimizu and Major Hayashi Yoshio, a representative of the Kwantung Army Headquarters, again visited Ma Zhanshan regarding the Jiang Bridge incident. They claimed to have received instructions from their government and the Kwantung Army Commander, stating that the Tao'an Railway had a loan relationship with the South Manchuria Railway and should be repaired by the South Manchuria Railway. They also planned to use military force to protect the work. Ma refuted this, stating that the South Manchuria Railway Bureau only had a creditor relationship with the Tao'an Railway. A creditor cannot repair a project on behalf of a debtor. Moreover, the Tao'an Railway was not under the jurisdiction of the Jiang Province government and could not agree to be repaired by the South Manchuria Railway. He would notify the Tao'an Railway Bureau to repair it themselves and not trouble the Japanese to interfere. The Japanese Consul and Major Hayashi still insisted on not agreeing, saying that it must be repaired by the Japanese. They also proposed four conditions: (1) The Nenjiang Bridge must not be used for war. (2) By noon on November 3rd, both the northern and southern armies must withdraw fifteen kilometers from the bridge. (3) The distance of the location, before the repair is completed, the two armies are not allowed to invade its territory. Once the repair is completed, the two armies will be notified again. (4) If the above requirements are not agreed to or hindered, it will be regarded as hostile to the Japanese army, and free action will be taken. At 4 p.m. that afternoon, two Japanese planes scouted the Jiang Bridge and Daxing Station area twice and dropped many leaflets.

On November 3rd, at 11 a.m., the Japanese army arrived at the Jiang Bridge with two armored trains, thirty soldiers, over a hundred South Manchuria Railway workers, and five planes, implementing the repair of the Jiang Bridge with military force. In order to avoid conflict, our army withdrew the few troops stationed at the Jiang Bridge to Daxing Station, fifteen kilometers away. However, when our army withdrew, the Japanese army threw a large number of bombs from the planes, injuring nine of our soldiers. At about 10 p.m., more than a hundred Japanese soldiers crossed the Jiang Bridge to the front line of our army, launching a fierce attack on us and throwing several bombs, injuring seven of our soldiers. After about two hours, because our side sought to avoid conflict and did not resist, the Japanese army retreated.

On November 4th, at 5 a.m., Major Hayashi of the Japanese army, accompanied by Mr. Hayazaki, a secretary from the Japanese Consulate, requested to go to the defense area of our army stationed at Daxing Railway Station to speak to our army. Shi Lanbin, Chief of Staff of the 3rd Infantry Brigade, agreed. At 8:10 a.m., they went to Harge Jiang Bridge from Jiang Province. Major Hayashi first addressed the Japanese soldiers west of the bridge. When Chief of Staff Shi was addressing our army, he forced Shi to sign a document admitting the withdrawal of our army and ordering its immediate execution. Chief of Staff Shi immediately refused, saying that he was the Chief of Staff of the 3rd Infantry Brigade and only a part of the staff. He could not order other troops in Jiang Province. Moreover, our soldiers were responsible for protecting the territory and overseas Chinese, which was legitimate defense, and others had no need to interfere. During the negotiations, Japanese soldiers had already advanced to our defense line and captured three of our soldiers. Although Chief of Staff Shi repeatedly negotiated based on reason, the result was that they were not released. It was heard from railway workers that the three soldiers captured by the Japanese had been killed by the Japanese army. On the same day, more than three hundred Japanese soldiers took advantage of the early morning fog to launch a fierce attack on our army. Our army did not engage with them. Unexpectedly, five Japanese planes again dropped six bombs on our army, injuring several soldiers and destroying Daxing Railway Station. Our army could no longer bear it and had to resort to legitimate defense. At 6 p.m., the Japanese army again used artillery fire to cover four thousand Japanese soldiers crossing the river, with dozens of mountain guns, seven planes, and four armored trains, advancing to Daxing Railway Station and launching a fierce attack on our army. Our officers and soldiers resisted to the death and were not subdued. Until dusk, the Japanese army's artillery fire continued unabated. Our army suffered more than five hundred casualties. The Jiang Province authorities, considering that the Daxing position was difficult to defend, ordered a retreat to Sanjianfang Railway Station (thirty miles from Daxing) at 2 p.m. on the 6th to defend the position. From the afternoon of the 6th, the Japanese army continued to attack us. (16th)

American Newspaper Warns Against Violent Japan

Yesterday's editorial in The Great American Evening News stated: "The reporter does not want to argue about defining war. Today, perhaps some still believe that there is no war in the three northeastern provinces, but from our perspective, there is already a war, and not a small-scale one. Ma Zhanshan, unafraid of a powerful enemy, has stepped forward to fight. Although he has not fought against the entire nation of Japan, he has already clashed with a part of the Japanese army and shown his good skills. We think that Ma's actions this time may cause the Japanese Empire to spend a huge amount of treasury funds. Japan can still not declare war on China, not declare war on General Ma. Japan can still call its dangerous and fortunate actions in the three northeastern provinces a business of maintaining peace, continuing to import its rifles, cannons, bombing planes, and other tools to maintain peace and order, until all the Chinese people in the three northeastern provinces are pacified and none are left, or all the Japanese residents in the three northeastern provinces are pacified and none are left, or both sides are severely injured, like tigers fighting in a village. From our perspective, perhaps the Japanese can do this. Today's situation seems that only the League of Nations can intervene to prevent the situation from erupting. However, the League of Nations seems to be in a difficult situation, at a loss and not knowing what to do. Soviet Russia is China's closest neighbor, but even if China-Russia relations are strong, we believe that Soviet Russia has sufficient common sense and thrift and is unwilling to participate in such a wasteful feast. Moreover, China and Russia have not yet resumed diplomatic relations. Japan can do whatever it wants at this time, but we really hope that it awakens from its delusion and examines reality. Even if it is late, it is not too late. If Japan does this, it is not pacifying the Northeast, but provoking the Northeast. It is not enough to protect Japanese residents, but makes the situation of Japanese residents more difficult. It is also not a way to increase the income of the South Manchuria Railway, but enough to promote its reduction. In short, Japan has made a big mistake. The only plan now is to clear the accounts, write off all previous events, practice the promises under the League of Nations Charter and the Anti-War Pact, and withdraw its troops. However, even if the Japanese hurry to withdraw their troops, it is still unknown whether this kind of tangled situation can be resolved satisfactorily after a long time of sorting out. If not, then we know that the stubbornness of the Japanese will cause huge losses to their own country and to the whole world."

Three-Year Economic Plan

▲ Chiang's Speech at the National Economic Council. At the first meeting of the National Economic Council held at the National Government on the 15th of this month, Chairman Chiang made an important report explaining the three-year economic plan. The full text of the speech is supplemented below: "Today is the inaugural meeting of the National Economic Council. On behalf of the council, I sincerely welcome all the committee members. The purpose of the establishment of this council is well known to all of you and need not be repeated. However, some of you may not be familiar with the work plan. I would like to explain the important points to all of you. The most important task of this council in the first phase is to set a three-year plan. Based on the various tasks that can develop the national economy, we will select the most needed ones and implement them in the near future, depending on the national financial resources. The first step is to select several of the most needed tasks and compile them into a definite plan. The second step is to identify the interrelationships of each plan and their communication methods. The third step is to determine their order of priority. Finally, we will determine a plan for the equal development of work within the three-year period. It will be implemented earnestly starting from the 21st year of the Republic of China. Regarding the financial aspect, it should first be decided by the Finance Committee recently established by the National Government how much funds the government can allocate each year for this construction. Then, this council will allocate the use of these funds. In addition to preparing the above-mentioned three-year plan, the current work of this council is to discuss the opinions contributed by various parties at any time, whether they are central, local, public or private organizations, or Chinese and foreign industrial, commercial, and financial institutions. All proposals will be studied by this council at any time and opinions will be expressed to collect the benefits of broad thinking. The existing proposals that can be used for the committee members to study are the guidance of the Huai River, land reclamation, the development of the Port of Greater Shanghai, the paving of the Nanjing-Shanghai automobile road, and the improvement of farmland, etc. Other industrial development plans that should be promoted by the government will also be submitted to this council for research and implementation. The second phase of the council's work is to determine a larger plan, planning the path that our country should follow in the development of the next ten years or so. The development of our country's industry should seek to be suitable for natural resources and local conditions. Therefore, the second phase of the plan should be based on the natural development of this industry, and the development of education and health systems should be used as a complementary element, with practical communication. The council is currently planning to expand the organization of the current preparatory office and recruit specialized talents in engineering, agriculture, health, education, and other fields to establish a strong secretariat. The secretariat of this council must not only be able to plan various tasks and submit them to this council for research and review, but also be able to take responsibility for assisting in the supervision of the implementation of the plan. Therefore, the selection of this personnel is very important. Furthermore, this council has agreed on cooperation methods with the technical departments of the League of Nations. Dr. Rajchman, the Director of the Health Section of the League of Nations, has stayed in China for several weeks and has made many plans for the technical cooperation between our country and the League of Nations. This council is very grateful for this. In the first month of the coming year, Mr. Haas, the Director of the Communications Section of the League of Nations, will also come to China to assist in the progress of all construction work of this council. I firmly believe that after the establishment of this council, all committee members will be able to express their honest opinions and jointly seek the progress of domestic construction undertakings. The future of the party and the country truly depends on this."

Surveying of the Huai River Embankment Project

▲ Two Teams Separately Survey the Upper and Lower Reaches ▲ North and South Embankments to be Built Simultaneously Bengbu Correspondence: The National Government Relief Flood Relief Association previously considered that the floods in the Huai River area in northern Anhui were particularly severe. In order to treat both the symptoms and the root causes, it purchased a large amount of American wheat and organized work relief. On the one hand, it repaired the Huai River embankment, and requested the Huai River Guidance Committee to dispatch surveying teams to conduct on-site sectional surveys. A few days ago, Sheng Dechun, the leader of the first surveying team of the Huai River embankment project, departed from Fengtai with his team to survey the upper reaches of the Huai River. He has surveyed to the Xiashankou and is currently surveying the Xifei River area. However, the bandit atmosphere is very strong in the upper reaches of the Fei River and above Zhengyangguan. It is not yet known whether it can be surveyed further forward. Yin Chengzhi, the leader of the second team, departed from Huaiyuan with his team to survey the lower reaches of the Huai River. Yesterday, they surveyed through Xinjiawan in Hebei, and have now surveyed to the Mo River Estuary in Fengyang County. They will soon survey to Linhuai Pass. It is recently heard that the National Government Relief Flood Relief Association still has a surplus after the distribution of relief food in northern Anhui. It plans to use work relief to build the south embankment at the same time as repairing the north embankment of the Huai River, to show equality and avoid regrets. A surveying team will soon be dispatched to survey the south bank of the Huai River and start construction on a regular basis. (18th)

Wuxi

Male and Female Double Suicide in Gongwei Hotel. The Gongwei Hotel on Gongyuan Road in the city received two people claiming to be Shanghai travelers, Gu Quansheng and a woman named Cai, on the afternoon of the 16th. They rented room number 19 and paid a dollar for the room. On the 18th, Gu Quansheng asked the tea room attendant, Guo A-Quan, where the post office was. After explaining the location, Gu was seen mailing a letter to Gu Xiutang in Songjiang. At the time, no one thought it was strange. Unexpectedly, at noon on the 19th, the travelers had not yet gotten up. They entered the room to check and saw the man and woman sleeping together, head to head, with cloth strips around their necks, appearing to have hanged themselves. They immediately reported to the Tu Zheng, Wu Shuntai, and at 5 p.m., reported to the County Court Procuratorate, requesting that someone be sent to examine the bodies.

Arrest of the Principal Offender in the Assault on Police and Resistance to Arrest Case. Meng Qingfa, a policeman from the 16th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, was beaten to death by gamblers while catching gamblers in the Zhu A-Da teahouse in Yangting Town, 8th District. Two accomplices, Zhu Zhongfen and Li Gengen, have been arrested and sent to the court for questioning and detention. It is learned that Director Hua of the Public Security Bureau is paying unusual attention to this case. Recently, it was discovered that the head of the teahouse, Zhu A-Da, had secretly returned home. He secretly ordered Xue Furui, the captain of the detective team, to order detectives Shen Minhua, Zai Shouquan, etc., to lead several detectives to the countryside.

To ambush and arrest him, and sure enough, Zhu A-Da was arrested. He was immediately taken to the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (19th) morning, Director Hua prepared a document and transferred him to the County Court. At 4 p.m., Chief Prosecutor Zhou opened the court, questioned him, and ordered him to be detained for further questioning and investigation.

Changzhou

Appropriation of Funds to Aid Ma Zhanshan. Wood industry colleagues from Jiangxi and Linqing, residing in Changzhou, were greatly moved by the fact that the violent Japan had forcibly occupied Liaoning and Jilin and was now eyeing Heilongjiang. Fortunately, General Ma Zhanshan disregarded his own safety and resisted to the death, finally defeating the fierce bandits. His loyalty and courage were commendable. They held a meeting the previous night to raise funds to help. Hu Youxian, Du Jiliang, and others pledged 1,000 yuan on the spot, which was wired free of charge to Heilongjiang Province through the Bank of China on the 18th. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association also appropriated 100 yuan, and a certain teacher donated 10 yuan from his savings, which were also remitted one after another.

Prosecutor Examines Murder Case. In Qianjia Village, near Hengshan Town, Fifth District, Wu County, Wang Bingsheng, a native of Jiangyin, about forty years old, suddenly died in a fish shed the night before. The nearby public security authorities reported to the County Court for an examination. The supervising prosecutor led his staff to examine the body on the 18th and found no injuries on the entire body. However, there was blood in the police gate and mouth. A silver needle was used to probe the front door, and it immediately turned black. It was determined that he had died from taking poison before his death. Yang Peikun, who was watching the fish shed, was taken to the city and will be investigated to determine the cause of death and further processed.

Jiangyin

Police Inspector Catches Gamblers, Conflicts with Civilian Police. Sun Zhili, director of the 5th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau in Shengang, received a report on the evening of the 16th that there was gambling at Jin Yuqi's house in X溝. He immediately ordered Police Inspector Ji Hou (from Xiangxiang, Hunan) to lead ten policemen to the scene. There were only several tables of mahjong. The civilian police therefore conflicted. Police Inspector Deng was injured, and patrolmen Sun Yihua, Wu Bingsheng, and Lu Tongzhang were also beaten, and two box cannons and seventy bullets were lost. Later, Ma A-chang and eleven others were apprehended at the Ma family mat. They were sent to the county on the afternoon of the 17th and interrogated by interrogator Wu Cheng. Jin Yuqi, Jin Gengen, Lin Masheng, and Yu Maxisheng, the heads of the gambling den, were taken into custody, and Ma A-chang and the other seven were released on bail pending the apprehension of the murderer Ma Shengyao and the instigator Cao Xiangfang for legal action.

Zhenjiang

Security Office Dispatches Troops to Huashan to Suppress Bandits. Bandits have suddenly risen in Huashan Town, Da Gang City, Zhenjiang Province, causing great disturbances. The Yangzhou Pacification Supervisor, Zeng, telegraphed Director Li of the Provincial Security Office, instructing him to immediately dispatch troops to suppress the bandits. After receiving the order, Director Li specially transferred troops yesterday to seize the opportunity to suppress the bandits, so as to pacify the local area.

Yangzhou

Telegraphic Order to Investigate Wrongful Imprisonment and Fraud Case. Pacification Supervisor Zhang Zhijiang, based on a report from Zhang Jibin, a citizen of Suqian County, accusing Qian Zhongkui of making false charges and dispatching troops to search and plunder property, and arresting his third younger brother Zhang Jipeng and fourth younger brother Zhang Min, detaining them in the regiment headquarters, and later demanding their release, transferred Zhang Jipeng and Zhang Min to the division headquarters, which was a wrongful imprisonment. He ordered the division commander, Zhang Huaying, to have Zhang Min, along with the plaintiff Qian Zhongkui, company commander Zhou Bingquan, all escorted to Yangzhou for interrogation to clarify the truth.

Teachers' Salary Demand Wave Expected to be Resolved. The Education Bureau of Jiangdu, because of salary arrears and strikes, assigned representatives to sit in the bureau and demand payment. Director Jia Qiheng, Supervisor Liu Yinnan, Section Chief Zi Xiufeng, Zhang Xuanqi, etc., specially went to the county to discuss the matter with County Chief Chen Nanxuan and Finance Bureau Chief Tong Maoke yesterday (17th), and first raised 3,000 yuan to return one-third of the salary arrears, so as to maintain the current situation and hope for an early resumption of classes.

Jiaxing

Record of a Robbery Encountered by the Jiahu Boat. The previous day (16th), the Jiahu transport boat encountered a robbery in Wangjiangjing, and fourteen passengers, both men and women, were kidnapped. This was recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that four of the female passengers and three of the male passengers have escaped. It is said that the bandit gang treated those they kidnapped fairly well, providing tea, water, and food. Their behavior and words were quite gentle, seemingly different from the usual so-called kidnappers. None of the kidnapped people were from the propertied class. Most of them were shop clerks. One named Sun Zhiyu used to work in a factory but has been unemployed for many years and is in a very difficult situation. Another, surnamed Zhou, from a village outside Nanxun shed, is now employed in a foreign goods store in Shanghai. Wu Weiru is an employee of the Nanxun Fuda Money Shop, and Wu Jimei is a trainee in a factory, all of whom have meager incomes. However, it is still unclear whether they have all been released or are still in danger.

Wangdian Apprehends Kidnappers. Xu Jinlan, a wealthy merchant in Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, was kidnapped by bandits on the evening of October 20 at a hotel at the Tangqiao head in the town and taken onto a boat. The town's water and land police sub-boats chased after them, and the bandits abandoned the boat and fled. The kidnapped person was rescued. The Wangdian water police and public security sub-bureau apprehended the bandit suspects Zheng A-lin, Shen Huaizhong, Shi Yongsheng, Zhou A-sheng, and Ni Rongsheng five days ago and sent them to the court with a document. After interrogation, Zheng A-lin confessed to the kidnapping and was ordered to be detained. The others were released on bail because there was no strong suspicion after interrogation, pending further questioning.

Hangzhou

Measures for Disposing of Confiscated Japanese Goods. The Hangzhou Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association stated that the number of Japanese goods seized and confiscated by the association's inspection team is gradually increasing, making it difficult to store them. Therefore, it has first formulated five measures for disposing of Japanese goods that are not easily stored: (1) Luxury goods will be burned in public. (2) Food and supplies will be distributed to disaster victims. (3) Explosive items will be sent to military agencies for use. (4) Medicines will be sent to public hospitals for medical use. (5) Raw materials will be distributed to engineering colleges or domestic goods factories to manufacture finished products separately. The above measures have been approved by the provincial party department for implementation.

Citywide Student Fundraising to Reward the Heilongjiang Army. All sectors of Hangzhou have stated that the military affairs in Heilongjiang are expanding daily and our army has repeatedly fought against the enemy. In addition to sending telegrams to Ma Zhanshan to express condolences, various telegrams have been sent to remit funds to reward the front-line soldiers. A decision was made to raise a huge amount of money again to continue to reward them in order to encourage morale. It was decided to rush to produce 300 donation registers and send them to the Hangzhou Municipal Education Bureau to order all levels of schools to unanimously set off on the 22nd with all students to raise donations, so that all the money could be remitted to Heilongjiang to reward the Heilongjiang army.

Ningbo

Pushing Sales of "Yinmen," Another Bloodshed Incident. The Tongfuchang and ten other fish shops in Ningbo previously purchased 240 pieces of "Sammon" from the British firm Anli Foreign Company in Shanghai, which were transported to Ningbo by the Xinjiangtian wheel. Because the public mistakenly thought it was Japanese fish, a major dispute occurred. After investigation by party and government agencies, it was learned that it was produced in Russia and allowed to be sold. The Tongfuchang goods store immediately set up a sales office in front of the Tianhou Palace in the city and hired Xiang Lianseng as the director of the sales office and Chen Ji as the legal advisor of the office. Until yesterday afternoon, patriotic workers He Shichang and others stated that the "Sammon" was very similar to Japanese fish, making it difficult for the public to identify it, which hindered anti-Japanese work. Therefore, they posted slogans everywhere urging people not to buy Japanese fish. When these slogans were posted near the sales area, they were seen by the store clerks, who reported it to the manager of the Tongfuchang store. The manager believed that the slogans posted by He Shichang and others, urging people not to buy Japanese fish, greatly impacted the sales of "Sammon." He immediately ordered the store clerks to use iron tools, wooden sticks, etc., to beat and injure He Shichang and others. He's head was broken by an iron tool, and he bled a lot. At that time, the audience believed that what the Tongfuchang fish store and others were selling was "Sammon" and that the slogans posted by He Shichang clearly stated Japanese fish. The store manager came out to interfere, which was tantamount to admitting that what he bought was Japanese fish. As a result, the crowd was greatly outraged and swarmed to the front of the sales office, smashing the signboard and throwing it into the river. The management personnel of the office knew that they had aroused public anger and fled one after another. Xiang, the director of the sales office, and Chen, the lawyer, were also denounced as profit-hungry running dogs.

Educational News

Important News

Ministry Order

Military Training Does Not Require Separate Uniforms ▲ Student Uniforms Applicable. The Ministry of Education stated that it had received a telegram from Cai Yuanze of the National Beiyang Institute of Technology stating that he had learned the instructions and announced that he would comply. However, he asked for instructions on whether the military training uniforms of all students in the institute should be paid for from the current account and issued by the school, or how they should be handled. The Ministry of Education instructed that the telegram had been received and that student uniforms should be used for military training and that there was no need to produce and distribute separate uniforms. He was ordered to comply.

Sichuan Province

Three Universities Merged and Renamed Sichuan University

▲ 600,000 Salt Funds Also Merged into the University. The Ministry of Education previously approved a telegram from Liu Wenhui, chairman of the Sichuan Provincial Government, stating that the merger of the three universities in Sichuan Province this time to establish a complete university is in line with the original plan of the Ministry, and should be handled in accordance with the University Organization Law and Regulations, so as to live up to the Ministry's grand intention to reorganize university education. The telegram stating the proposed situation has been reached, and it is hoped that it will be reviewed and implemented. The compilation of the merger has already begun. The proposed name of the school is National Sichuan University, and it is requested that it be approved for filing. Furthermore, the annual funding for Chengdu University is 600,000 yuan drawn from the Sichuan salt funds. It is proposed to transfer this to the National Sichuan University as funding, and it is requested that a final decision be made, and that the Ministry of Finance be consulted for reference. The Ministry of Education replied that the proposed name of the National Sichuan University and the transfer of Chengdu University's salt funds to the National Sichuan University should be approved for filing. A special reply has been sent in addition to forwarding it to the Ministry of Finance.

Suzhou Middle School Normal Department will be responsible for convening the meeting. Shanghai Middle School Rural Normal School will be responsible for convening the meeting. Zhenjiang Middle School Normal Department and Songjiang Women's Middle School Normal Department were elected as alternate Executive Committee members. The distribution of duties among the Executive Committee members is as follows: Standing Committee: Suzhou Women's Middle School Normal Department; Research: Suzhou Middle School Normal Department; Suzhou Rural Normal School; Publicity: Shanghai Middle School Normal Department; Taizhou Middle School Normal Department.

▲ Opinions of the Jiangsu Province Normal Department Federation on the Ministry of Education's Revised Curriculum for Senior High School Normal Departments: (1) The workload of courses in the sixth semester should be reduced, and emphasis should be placed on practical training. (2) Increase credits for Chinese Language and National Language: 5 hours per week for each year in the first and second academic years, 4 credits; 4 hours per week, 4 credits, in the first semester of the third academic year (including 2 hours, 2 credits for National Phonetics); elective course in Philology. (3) In the science curriculum outline, topics such as astronomy, meteorology, and geology should be taught with emphasis on methods and should be coordinated with manual arts classes to facilitate the creation of simple instruments. (4) The content of the geography curriculum should include regional geography in addition to various issues relating to the country, in order to supplement the deficiencies of junior high school (can be based on Zhang Qizhao's edited "New School System Senior High School Textbook: National Geography," dividing the country into thirty-three natural regions); the foreign content, in addition to various issues, should also include regional geography to supplement the deficiencies of junior high school (can be based on RUSSELL SMITH HUMAN GEOGTAPHY BOOK IT). (5) Primary school administration is moved to the fifth semester. (6) Educational psychology is set at 6 credits: 3 credits for child psychology and 3 credits for learning psychology, moved to the first academic year; the part on scholastic psychology is moved to primary school teaching methods. (7) A section on "research methods" and children's morality should be added to the curriculum outline for child psychology within educational psychology. (8) Educational testing and statistics are changed to 4 credits; the curriculum outline should include "experimental education methods." (9) Elective educational history is 4 credits, including modern educational trends. (10) Logic is moved to the second academic year. (11) "Internship Commencement" begins in the fourth semester, with the fourth and fifth semesters each accounting for one-sixth of the total internship credits, and the sixth semester accounting for three-fifths of the total internship credits. (12) Internship credits and time should be redistributed. (13) Internships should be based on the entire teaching process as a unit, not on the nature of the subject.

▲ Training Standards for Normal School Students (Drafted by the Jiangsu Province Normal Department Federation): 1. Beliefs: (1) Firmly believe that the Three Principles of the People are the only doctrine for saving the country; (2) Firmly believe that education is a tool for saving the country; (3) Firmly believe that serving primary school education is our lifelong career. 2. Physical Fitness: (1) Have a healthy and strong physique; (2) Have a spirit of perseverance and hard work. 3. Knowledge: (1) Have a wealth of common knowledge; (2) Have a scientific mind; (3) Have an interest in research. 4. Skills: (1) Have production skills; (2) Have skills in teaching children; (3) Have skills in guiding society. 5. Conduct: (1) Thinking must be revolutionary; (2) Actions must be disciplined; (3) Attitude must be childlike; (4) Life must be labor-oriented. (End)

Local News

Anti-Japanese Associations of Various Universities

Donations to Aid Heilongjiang Yesterday Were Very Successful ▲ Over 10,000 People Departed from More Than 30 Schools

▲ Economic Committee to Meet Today to Discuss Methods

Emergency Cadre Meeting Convened This Afternoon

The United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of students from various universities in this city, after a resolution passed by the representative assembly on the 17th of this month to hold a general fundraising and publicity campaign on the 19th and 20th, immediately notified all schools to actively prepare. According to investigations, approximately 30 schools with a total of over 10,000 people departed yesterday. Each team consisted of about 10 people, carrying their respective school flags and symbols, intercepting passersby along the way, and soliciting donations. Those who donated were very enthusiastic, so yesterday's results were quite good. The donation cards were printed with the words "Shanghai University Students' United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association thanks the soldiers of Heilongjiang." Those who donated between 20 cents and one yuan were given a white card, and those who donated more than one yuan were given a yellow card. How the funds raised will be handled and remitted to the Northeast is still under serious consideration. Therefore, it has been decided to convene the Economic Committee at 10:00 AM today (the 20th) to discuss various methods. Attendees will be from the School of Law and Political Science, Soochow University, Shanghai University, Jinan University, Great China University, Guanghua University, China Public School, and other schools. It is also heard that the 17th Emergency Cadre Meeting will be held at 1:00 PM today to discuss all important pending matters, etc.

▲ Notice from the United Association: To whom it may concern, it is hereby announced that an emergency representative assembly will be held at 2:00 PM on the 20th of this month to discuss serious current affairs matters. It is hoped that your school's representative will attend on time without delay. Respectfully addressed to all school anti-Japanese national salvation associations.

▲ Statement from the United Association: To whom it may concern, having read in your newspaper that the 12th representative assembly of this association rescinded the resolution on the cadre committee and the suspension of classes, and that the publicity and fundraising were done in spare time, this is completely inconsistent with the facts. This is likely a mistake by the reporter from the Kuomintang News Agency. An investigation shows that items 2 and 3 of the resolution of the 12th representative assembly of this association were for the suspension of classes for publicity and fundraising on the 19th and 20th, and there was no rescission of the suspension of classes. This letter is specially sent to request a correction. Respectfully addressed to the chief editor of Shen Bao, Shanghai University Students' United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association.

Various Schools Donate to Ma Zhanshan in Support of Anti-Japanese Efforts

▲ Jinan University All teachers, students, and staff of the National Jinan University were moved by General Ma's brave fight against the invaders and unanimously made donations. Yesterday, a telegram was sent, stating: "Chairman Ma Zhanshan of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, your meritorious service in standing firm despite the invasion by the tyrannical Japanese has been deeply felt throughout the country. General, though far away in the remote wilderness, your lone army defies the enemy at the border, your prestige shines, and the enemy's courage is chilled. Not only does the entire country admire you, but you have also brought glory to our nation. The entire school, gazing afar, has nothing to offer in tribute. Therefore, we have collected a small sum and will immediately wire two thousand yuan to reward the troops and express our humble intentions. We hope that the General will continue to make persistent efforts, kill all the enemies, glorify our Chinese spirit, and secure our borders. Your loyal servant, National Jinan University, all teachers, students, and staff, two thousand people, respectfully send our greetings."

▲ Fudan University The students of this university sent an urgent telegram, stating: "To all newspaper offices and elders, brothers, and sisters throughout the country: The Japanese bandits have invaded and occupied our land for no reason, slaughtering our people. Our country has repeatedly made concessions, but they have taken an inch and want a mile. Right and wrong are clearly distinguished. The United States is the country that upholds the Washington Treaty and initiated the Kellogg-Briand Pact. If it still holds true to justice, how should it speak out and take effective measures to punish the Japanese bandits and maintain world peace? However, after reading the newspaper, we learned that the United States actually compromised with the Japanese bandits and proposed a so-called 'conciliation plan,' hoping that China would make further concessions. This is absurd and outrageous. The imperialists' intention to conspire to harm us is already clearly revealed. All of our citizens should now be truly aware and seek liberation through self-reliance. We vow to oppose all so-called conciliation plans and any policies involving the partition and joint control of China until our last breath. The future of the nation truly depends on this. The Shanghai Fudan University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association respectfully sends our greetings."

▲ Nanyang Business College All teachers and students of the Nanyang Senior Commercial Middle School launched a donation campaign to provide military pay for the brave soldiers of Heilongjiang. The previous day, they entrusted 200 yuan to the local Life Weekly magazine to remit on their behalf. Yesterday, the students continued to pledge donations, reaching another 200 yuan. It is heard that the school also telegraphed the Fourth National Congress in Nanjing, requesting the government to quickly send Zhang Fakui's entire army to aid Heilongjiang. The telegram briefly stated, "This can not only live up to General Ma's loyalty but also fulfill Commander Zhang's ambition." The words were extremely tragic and sincere.

▲ Jiaotong University Jiaotong University sent a telegram, stating: "Chairman Ma of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, you have repeatedly defeated the Japanese bandits and demonstrated your public loyalty. We respectfully collect funds from teachers and students and together present a cup of water to the soldiers, donating 1,500 yuan to help with military pay, to be remitted through the Bank of China, to boost morale, and await the triumphant return. All faculty, staff, and students of Shanghai Jiaotong University respectfully send our greetings."

Fudan Students Prepare to Go to the Northeast

Fudan University The entire student body, filled with righteous indignation and boiling with passion, felt that the tyrannical Japanese had long occupied Liaoning and Jilin and were now trying to seize Heilongjiang. They felt particularly tragic and moving towards Ma Zhanshan's lone army resisting with all its strength, and they were eager to rise up. As soon as preparations are complete, they will depart for the Northeast, vowing to kill the great enemy together with their blood. Shanghai Teachers and Staff Anti-Japanese

National Salvation Association Raises Funds to Assist General Ma

The Shanghai Teachers and Staff Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, believing that General Ma Zhanshan is loyal and brave in defending the country and avenging the humiliation of his compatriots, held its third executive committee meeting on the 18th of this month and decided to raise funds for assistance. The measures are extracted as follows: Announce in the newspaper to all teachers and staff of public and private schools at all levels in this city to donate 3% of one month's salary to assist General Ma Zhanshan. All funds should be remitted by each school directly to Qiqihar, Heilongjiang, before the 25th of this month, and the amount remitted should be notified to this association for compilation and public announcement in the newspaper. All schools are requested to proceed with this fundraising and assistance immediately. Signed by Executive Committee members Huang Zaoxiong, Zhou Feicheng, Wu Xiu, Wang Dingcheng, Chen Jicheng, Wang Junyao, Dai Yuheng, Zheng Shaoqing, Zhang Zaibo, Cheng Minkai, Feng Fusheng, Kong Fanxi, Xu Zeye, Wu Zijiu, Hu Shuhua, Cheng Kuanzheng, Lu Yuanhu, Tao Baichuan, Lü Xintian, Yang Demin, Wang Xiaoying, Ma Jiazhen, Zhao Lüqing, Tong Hangbai, Shen Tianbai, Guo Weiping, Tang Xianghou, Zhou Darong, Zhang Wanqing, Yu Nanqiu, Wang Wujun, Zhang Yongchun.

Telegram to Chairman Jiang and Vice Commander Zhang To Chairman Jiang of the Nanjing National Government and Vice Commander Zhang in Beiping: The border officials of the tyrannical Japanese have failed in their duty. In less than two days, thousands of miles of land have been lost. This has never been heard of in history. Now, Chairman Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang Province, with a small force, resists the enemy with skill and is still able to capture generals and raise flags, chasing and driving back the enemy. His morale is high, his righteousness is commendable, and we have repeatedly heard news of victories, which the whole country celebrates. However, it is a common truth that few can defeat many, and we fear that his force is small, his supplies are lacking, and setbacks are possible. If Heilongjiang is unfortunately lost again, Zhili and Shandong will also fall. Therefore, we urgently telegraph you, requesting that you quickly send elite reinforcements, provide sufficient supplies and equipment, and order Chairman Ma to take full authority to incorporate the retreating troops from Liaoning and Jilin to increase his strength, so as to protect the territory and recover the lost land. In haste, we await your orders with great anxiety.

Telegram to General Ma Zhanshan To Chairman Ma and all soldiers in Qiqihar, Heilongjiang: The tyrannical Japanese have invaded and occupied our Liaoning and Jilin and are now coveting Heilongjiang. Fortunately, our chairman commands with skill, morale is high, and the lone army fights bravely to protect our territory, win glory for the country, and avenge the humiliation of our compatriots. Your loyalty and bravery are commendable. Looking north, we deeply admire you. Our association, in addition to raising funds to assist the troops, has telegraphed Chairman Jiang and Vice Commander Zhang, requesting that they quickly send elite reinforcements and provide sufficient supplies and equipment. We specially telegraph our condolences, hoping that you will continue to fight for final victory. The compatriots in the educational circles of this city vow to be your backing. In haste, we send our telegram with tears, hoping that you will take it into consideration. Executive Committee of the Shanghai Teachers and Staff Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association.

Free Talk

Recollections from the Dai Liang (Tortoiseshell Beam)

— Yanzi

After the Red Sheep Calamity, the war between the Han people continued. Surpassing the Eight Banners, only the General of Jilin, Yitang'a, was brave and skilled in battle, unparalleled in 情　. The troops under his command were all valiant soldiers, safeguarding the Northeast. The Qing court relied heavily on him. When the Sino-Japanese War broke out, Yitang'a led his ten thousand-plus men, disregarding the troops under Wu Dacheng. He fought fiercely in the area of ​​Gai County's Mount Motianling, repeatedly using ingenious tactics to lure the Japanese army deep into strategic locations, gathering them together to annihilate them. Having gone through dozens of battles, he always took the lead, charging into the enemy lines, engaging in close hand-to-hand combat. Those who stood in his way were routed. When Wu Dacheng's troops were stationed in Jinzhou, Wu personally led the central army, Song Qing was on the right flank, and Yitang'a led the Eight Banners soldiers on the left flank. The Japanese General Ōshima Yoshimasa knew that Yitang'a and Song Qing were not to be trifled with, so he used light cavalry to intercept the central army, with mixed results. When Wu's main camp was routed and retreated into Guanzhong, the ones who supported him were Yitang'a and Song Qing. Song was experienced and prudent, using offense as defense, while Yitang'a defended strategic locations and choked off the enemy, even using light cavalry to outflank the enemy army, attacking from three sides. His battle merits were particularly outstanding. In the Battle of Mount Motianling, it was late at night and raining heavily. Yitang'a attacked them unprepared, selecting eight hundred cavalry soldiers, biting their mouthpieces, and rushing into the enemy camp. Yitang'a rode a furious horse, commanding and beheading over a thousand, capturing five hundred enemy soldiers. Corpses lay everywhere, and blood flowed like a canal. The Japanese army retreated more than fifty li, and before they could catch their breath, Song's army arrived and defeated the Japanese army. In this battle, Yitang'a seized more than four thousand guns and twenty cannons. Yitang'a reported the victory to the Qing court, declaring his intent to strike straight into Huanglong (the enemy's lair) and wipe out the enemy. Public opinion praised him. How could the court be filled with fear, eager to negotiate peace? The Governor-General of Zhili, Li Hongzhang, was ordered to go to Maguan to negotiate peace, and the two armies ceased fighting. Yitang'a resigned due to the peace, but the Emperor ordered him to stay. Yitang'a still returned to Jilin to cultivate, leading to the loss of this great opportunity. Speaking of it cannot help but make people feel regret.

Trivial Tales of the Japanese Nation

— Zheng Yimei

Since the Shenyang Incident, everyone in the country has been paying attention to and exploring the situation in Japan. Now, I will describe what I heard from my Japanese friends on the left.

All Japanese people over the age of 21 have the obligation to serve as soldiers. Once the country has war, the scholars will stop studying and the farmers will stop farming. Industrialists and businessmen will stop their work to go. Even in times of peace, they must practice combat and lead a military life. Therefore, for those seeking employment, the other party must ask whether they have ever joined the army and examine their certificates. Otherwise, they will be rejected as fugitives and will not be accepted.

Excluding Chinese people is a common practice in Japan, and it has not started today. The reason is that mixed residence is the only right of equal countries. China cannot be in an equal position with Japan, so it cannot give China the right to mixed residence. Moreover, it refers to Chinese people as people of the lower class of society, and most of them have not been educated. Mixed residence may hinder the customs and hygiene of Japan. Chinese people are stingy by nature and are good at accumulating wealth, so they are afraid of taking huge amounts of money back to their country, which may hinder the economy of Japan. Chinese people have a low standard of living, and the wages are low. In comparison, everyone is happy to use cheap Chinese labor, which hinders the lives of Japanese laborers.

Japanese people can imitate various Western utensils and textiles, and they are cheaper than Western goods. Therefore, Japanese people are happy to use domestic goods, hold them constantly and keep it a habit. It is not like our country's great pain, and then we start to talk about boycotting and promoting it. Just a short time of five minutes.

Japanese culture uses our country's culture as its culture. Famous books in our country are translated into Japanese texts. Such as the Four Books and Five Classics, Zhuangzi, Laozi, Liezi, Xunzi, Mozi, Guanzi, Han Feizi, and other masters, as well as the prose of the Eight Great Masters, the poems, songs, and ballads of the Tang, Song, and Yuan dynasties, and the words of novelists, Romance of the Three Kingdoms, Dream of the Red Chamber, Scholars, Journey to the West. Flowers in the Mirror and Traces of Flower and Moon are all made into Japanese and sold in workshops. Every household is reciting. Called Chinese Studies. Now that the war has broken out, a newspaper in Japan specializes in translating the major military and national affairs published in our country's newspapers.

Song of the Brave Soldiers of Shuofang

— He Tianjian

After the violent sun invaded my Shenyang and Jilin, it further planned to invade my Heilongjiang Province. Unexpectedly, it was repeatedly defeated by my Heilongjiang Army and the reclamation army. The violent sun's court and the public were disturbed by this. It will besiege with a large army, but the weather is cold and the ice is frozen, and the isolated army is trapped and defended. I have not yet heard of any support from our side, and the granary is empty. What can be done? General Ma has done his best to defend the territory, and the righteous men under his command are also united in hatred and can wash away the national shame for the country. It is also a strong city for our country to last forever. I am deeply grateful that people across the country have automatically donated large sums of money in recent days. I hope that our calligraphy and painting circles will also rise up and plan for it. So that General Ma and all righteous men can complete their meritorious deeds of defending against insult. I hereby compose this song to inspire it.

Shenyang has been trapped for two months, and the debate is endless. Jing Tang was coerced and pitied the young children. Mock at the old fool who claims to be loyal. The way to destroy Korea is to destroy my country. I don't know what use is the raising of a million soldiers. Sitting and making the mountains and rivers end like this. I didn't expect that there was still a man named Ma, whose heart was like iron and whose spirit was like a rainbow. He raised his arms and called for national disaster, and each man had the courage of ten thousand men. The Battle of Nenjiang broke the enemy's courage, like a defeated leaf destroying a strong wind. The Japanese court and the public were shocked when they heard the news, and the whole island was the same. They even sent out troops to support them, and they will gather a large army in Manchuria and Mongolia. An isolated army is deeply trapped, what can I do? The tragic people are still singing and dancing. You don't see the north wind sweeping the ground like a sharp arrow, and it is difficult to keep warm when sandwiched with cotton. You don't see the enemy in the ice and snow, and the hungry body and cold body are wielding swords. You must know what hard work is for, and you will protect the mountains and rivers with iron and blood. Alas, I will protect the mountains and rivers with iron and blood.

The reason for this is to peek at a glimpse of public opinion in our country and the state of the military situation, so as to inform its people of the conspiracy against me.

The Japanese army is arrogant and invincible. A certain celebrity was worried about it. He once published a paper, roughly saying that soldiers are too proud, which will lead to defeat, and pointed out that the Japanese army has not experienced a formal war since the Russo-Japanese War. Since the revolution, Chinese warlords have been fighting endlessly for twenty years. On the one hand, it is enough to consume China's strength, and on the other hand, it is enough to enrich the military's battlefield experience. Therefore, the outbreak of this incident is not optimistic in Japan. That celebrity is really a knowledgeable person. Our country should work hard for it. There is hope of attacking Fusang in the east.

Viewing the Modern Famous Painting Exhibition

— Yu Kun

Mr. Xue Baolun gathered modern painting exhibitions by forty famous artists at the Ningbo Fellow Association. The grand occasion can be said to be unprecedented since the National Art Exhibition. And the exquisite examination of the exhibits also surpasses it. The most famous products of the whole exhibition are the reputations of Mr. Fu Tienian, Zheng Wuchang, Qian Shoutie, and Chen Xiaodie. Tienian has been away from Beiping for a long time, and Shanghai people are eager for his works. Therefore, on the first day of the exhibition, it was already booked and empty. Especially a mo-orchid painting, the rhyme is superb. And Mr. Chen Xiaodie's large-scale lotus flower is only a remnant lotus on the paper. The style is charming, especially above Tienian's ink orchid. Qian Shoutie has four ink-painting flowers, which can directly compete with Yu Ji. It is appropriate that there are always people standing in front of these paintings. Mr. Wu Dongmai said that watching Xiaodie's flower paintings, the brush and ink are elegant, which can make all the works in the field have the regret of too much vermilion and too much ink. I said that modern painters lack authors in terms of skill. If we talk about natural talent and ingenuity, then Dieye's (Xiaodie's other name) recent works, even Hu Fan, cannot surpass them. Mr. Wu Hufan never allows people to paint. But only for Xiaodie's recent works, he said, "Fairy, fairy." Its value can be imagined. Shoutie's paintings have been expensive in Dongying for a long time. Recently, because of Japan's atrocities, he vowed never to sell his works to the Japanese again. His character is like this. His paintings have a magnificent atmosphere. Zheng Wuchang and He Tianjian's works are all carefully managed. The layout is new and chic. The use of the brush is unrestrained. The two gentlemen have many disciples. Therefore, the recent art world has gradually abandoned the unrestrained style of Anji and tended to be pure. Therefore, Zheng He's contribution to the art world is not shallow. Looking at the exhibits in the whole exhibition, most of them are fresh and elegant. There are very few people who scribble wildly with cinnabar ink. It has already changed the style of the vertical and horizontal painters two or three years ago. The ancients said, "Looking at the style of painting at a time, you can spy on the subtle changes in the rule and chaos of the times." Is it not far away from the world to rule? I look forward to it. So I am happy to write it down.

There Are Only Two Generals in the Republic of China

— Da Shuan

The rich forest and fertile plains of Northeast China are full of treasures. Since September 18, the dwarfish slaves invaded. In a few hours, the bandits did not shed blood and settled by spreading the news. The Black Mountain collapsed and the White Water Zhu Yin. The young officer said, "Do not resist." The revolutionary government also said, "Be calm." But begging for help from the League of Nations, the people of the country also followed and feared it. Suspecting that the Japanese bandits descended from the sky, they all have three heads and six arms.

The wind is sad and the border is isolated. General Ma only knows that he has a responsibility to defend the soldiers and is not succumbed by the bandit's edict. With thousands of people, he is trapped in a corner. There is no support army behind him, and he is fighting a death battle with the violent bandits. The bandits were repeatedly defeated. The people of the country suspected that the bandits had three heads and six arms. Now they suddenly realized that they were silver-like wax and not enough to strike. With the knowledge of the revolutionary government and young officers, how could they not know and be detailed? But they were frightened by false rumors and collapsed when they saw the wind. Could it be that they have other intentions? The people of the country are stupid and foolish, and how can they measure their profoundness? However, the people of the country are shaking and about to fall into the cave of slaves of the subjugated country in terror. The time for two months is really worrying like burning, and the day is like a year. The government and young officers are still as calm as ever. In the past 20 years, China has only blocked Russia and defended it. It can be called a war. In the past 20 years, only Han Guangdi and Ma Zhanshan can be called generals. General Han died in battle and sacrificed his country. Only General Ma Zhanshan is trapped in the border and supports this half of the broken country. I am afraid for the general, and I am afraid for the people of the country. (Transfer to pay for disaster relief)

Records of Sights and Sounds of the Old Capital

— Zhu An

During the Qianlong period of Changdian, the tomb of Li Neizhen, a historian of the Liao Dynasty, was discovered in the east of Liulichang. There is a saying in its Zhizhi stone that it was buried in Haiwang Village in the east of the city. Then I realized that Liulichang was the eastern suburb during the Khitan period. Liulichang is the place where the Ministry of Industry set up to make glazed bricks and tiles. The whole street is bookstores, antique shops and South paper shops, such as firework restaurants, which are only occasionally seen. Since Daoxian, the husbands of the Jixiang family have been reviewing books, appreciating calligraphy and painting, and stroking Yi Ding in their spare time to spend their leisurely years. Implicitly forming the cultural center of Beidu. At the beginning of the Lunar New Year, vendors set up stalls among them. The road is blocked for it. The police station must first specify the route to clear the vehicles and horses. Only then can we be safe. It is said that no one in the whole city, rich or poor, elegant or vulgar, male or female, old or young, Chinese or foreign, does not want to visit and enjoy it. It is called visiting Changdian. After the seventeenth year, the Lunar New Year was banned, and it declined slightly. However, it was restored as usual. It is said that the prosperity of the old capital cannot but rely on this.

There was a man named Wang Zhuoran who investigated Changdian Commercial from the third day of the first lunar month to the fifteenth day of the Republic of China for ten years. He made eight tables. One day of important goods refers to children's toys. It is the best in various businesses. The daily sales are more than 80,000 copper coins. The second is food and drink, which refers to tea and snacks. The third is daily necessities, mostly women's makeup. The fourth is antiques, including 139 antique shops, 50 antique painting shops, and 28 ancient book shops. The fifth is miscellaneous items, such as firecrackers and goldfish. The sixth is stunts, such as the Western Mirror. The seventh is gambling, which is divided into drawing lots, rolling eggs, and turning around. The eighth is non-commercial business, which is the amusement fair exhibition hall, etc., operated by the government and schools.

Hu Yinglin's Shao Shi Shan Fang Ji of the Ming Dynasty said that the bookstores in Yan are mostly on the right of Damingmen and outside the Ministry of Rites and on the west of Gongchenmen. Every time the conference tries the candidates, the bookstores are listed in front of Yang. Every time after the Flower Dynasty, two or three days later, they moved to Dengjin. Every time on the first and last days of the month, they moved to the City God Temple. Deng City is the farthest east and the City God Temple is the farthest west. They are all places for trade during the day. Deng City is three days a year, and the City God Temple is three days a month. When the period comes, all kinds of goods gather there, and books are one of them. This is the situation of selling books in the Ming Dynasty, which is very different from today. Today, in addition to Liulichang and its vicinity, there are the most bookstores in Longfu Temple. There are also small markets in Hair Hutong, but the quality is slightly lower. In recent years, the bookstores in Dong'an Market are lined up, mostly new books for ordinary students to browse. The hundred industries in the old capital are declining, but the old book industry is developing more and more. It is said that learning is prosperous and the needs are more and more. Books that were previously unpopular and no one cared about are now regarded as professional careers. For example, local chronicles of various provinces used to be bought by the pound, but now each copy is worth several yuan. Rare ones are worth hundreds of yuan. Genealogy books were not included in the collection. Now they are also collected in the Beijing Library, but they are still suffering from nowhere to find them. In addition, there are specially stationed personnel in Japan, Europe and the United States. They are busy searching for them every day and are willing to pay a lot of money. There are also domestic good-natured people who have a lot of money to compete for good books. They communicate with each other and respond to each other. They all regard Beijing as the area of ​​Wan Gu. Liulichang and Longfu Temple have branches stationed in various places with cadres. They are still worried that the response is not enough. In recent years, the collections of old families in the city have been dug up, but there are still treasures that have not been discovered in remote areas of the outer counties. Although people in the bookstores are ignorant of the source of knowledge, they know the names and versions like treasures. If they want to find a book, they can just tell one store. They can turn around and search for it to report. Even if they stop and do not buy, they will not complain. The items displayed in the annual Changdian New Year are not necessarily of the highest quality. People who like to spend time and eliminate time beside the cold stalls may occasionally get a fragmented book at a low price. If you really want to buy a book, you don't have to stick to this time. The same is true for buying antiques and calligraphy and paintings.

Fullness invites loss. A drunk fool is born. One day he was in a mysterious state and heard the conversation between A and B. He felt that it was humorous and interesting, so he specially recorded it.

A said, "This time the violent sun is acting as the host and forcibly occupying my Northeast. All the losses suffered by our country are really countless. It just corresponds to the saying in the book "Fullness invites loss."

"Full" is Manchuria, of course referring to the Northeast, and the word "invite" contains the meaning of inducement. Because the Northeast is rich in resources and the benefits are everywhere, the Japanese see it and covet it. Therefore, they rush to it and keep saying "Protecting the interests of Manchuria and Mongolia" to carry out various acts of aggression, resulting in today's losses. The ancients predicted it with clever words and puns. It has long been revealed in advance. It is a pity that the person with the responsibility of defending the territory has not read much and does not know the true meaning of it. Otherwise, if he thinks about the danger and prevents it in advance, how could he lose the territory and humiliate the country and ruin it?

B said, "He (referring to the person with the responsibility of defending the territory) did not read books. However, he did not understand what he read. What he read was only the sentence "Humility benefits." He thought he was a humble gentleman and that suffering a loss was a bargain. This is what is called "Humility benefits," so when he encountered enemy soldiers approaching the border, he also took humility as his principle, holding the non-resistance doctrine and retreating step by step. People could get it without effort. In the past, Zhao Pu used half a book of Analects to govern the world. Now he has ruined the Northeast by misreading a sentence of the book. It is so sad.

Saying Department Decision Wheel Club

A Countryman Comes to Shanghai Again (Twenty-Two)

— Bao Tianxiao

At that time, the countrymen did not understand how trampling out a group of their fire was considered touching their bad luck, and how burning a group of messy paper on fire was considered burning the road. He wanted to ask the friend who helped him out of the siege about this question.

That friend was very honest and told the countrymen.

"This is a superstition of the lower classes of society in Shanghai. For example, a rickshaw puller drags his rickshaw out and touts it for a long time without finding a passenger. He will burn the road. He burns a piece of paper vigorously and smokes it randomly in front and behind the rickshaw. Those who sell five-spice tea eggs, those who sell white sugar lotus porridge, those who sell osmanthus fat cake, and those who sell ham bean paste dumplings, all small businesses who cannot find customers, they are also anxious and burn a piece of paper vigorously and smoke it randomly in front and behind their burdens and baskets and all their business tools. Sometimes they also silently communicate with the gods and pray. This is considered burning the road. Those prostitutes are also like this. They cannot live without pulling a customer every day. Some of them do not own their bodies. They call it begging for a body. If they cannot pull a customer back at night, they will be beaten and scolded. So they are anxious and think that their luck has not been good these two days, so they often burn the road like rickshaw pullers and small businesses. Those rickshaw pullers and small businesses burn a piece of paper vigorously and smoke it randomly in front and behind their rickshaws or in front and behind their burdens and baskets and all their business tools. Those prostitutes are pitiful because they do not have any business tools. Their business tool is their body and all and part of their body. So they burn a piece of paper vigorously and smoke it randomly inside their crotch. This is their burning the road. I did not expect you, old gentleman, to misunderstand and trample out the remaining fire on their paper, so it is considered touching their bad luck." "In this way, these girls who are prostitutes also feel very pitiful." The countrymen immediately felt sympathy for these prostitutes. In the past, people who wrote poems had two lines of poetry saying, "People say this is a pair of mandarin ducks, but I look at them as mourning geese." Although the countrymen cannot write poetry, they are very rich in that kind of poetic meaning.

"Isn't it? You see that although they are dressed up enchantingly on the outside, they are actually very miserable. There are also many who have venereal diseases and have to come out to solicit customers. If you come into contact with them, you will become an old milk shed or a fruit store clerk tomorrow when you go back."

"What is a milk shed? What is a fruit store?" The countrymen did not understand this kind of hidden language.

"Haha, a milk shed is gonorrhea, and a fruit store is simply selling syphilis."

Commercial News

Finance

The gold standard rebounded and fell

▲ Weak drop of more than eighteen taels ▲ Panic spreads frequently and huge changes are discovered Yesterday, the gold standard still had huge changes, with crazy winds and raging waves causing horror. The rise and fall of more than ten taels was impossible to deal with. The total turnover in the front and back markets was twenty-three or four taels. Looking back, it finally fell by more than eighteen taels. This is a reverse direction after many days of consecutive rises. The requests for supply from various companies are still very different. However, people's hearts have turned from firm to empty. Although the silver market has fallen, it is not affected. The reason is that the private telegram has not moved. The initial opening fell back. Later, it broke through 660 taels. It was followed by the tightening of the exchange rate. The big players in the market have always bought in, showing a sharp edge. There were almost a crowd of rising suns who suddenly rushed out seventy taels. Unfortunately, bad news came, the violent sun attacked black intensely, and the exchange rate saw a relaxation. Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a generally flat to weak hovering trend across all months after the opening in the morning and afternoon. Textiles

Local Products Unable to Meet Demand

The textile market remains sluggish, with a very quiet atmosphere. Western goods are lacking in inventory, and ordinary goods are extremely scarce. Eastern goods are being boycotted, and local products are unable to meet demand, often resulting in stockouts. Even the long-term orders of various factories have been completely filled. The positive trend is unprecedented, and profits can be guaranteed. There is no shortage of people preparing to organize and set up factories. This is a good phenomenon amid the promotion of domestic goods. Therefore, even if lower-quality goods were to be cleared, they would likely suffer a severe setback. Among the local products, the most recent ones are velvet goods. Double-width thick velvet from Tongcheng is priced at 9 qian and 7.5 fen, single-width from various factories at 4 qian and 7.5 fen, and high-quality striped velvet at 9 taels, with ordinary velvet at 8 taels and 1 qian. The production of wool velvet is also increasing, with prices quoted at 3 qian and 2 fen and 3 qian. Bleached velvet is being snapped up by napping factories, and Sanlu and Santao loose goods have been quoted at around 4 qian, mainly because there is a lack of spot goods. Fei Fa velvet and Yuehua velvet can also be spun. Fine serge and gong ni production are increasing daily. Cotton cloth remains stable, with 11-pound Sanlu and Santu both at 5 taels and 5 qian, and 9-pound Mao Ying at 5 taels and 2 qian. Fine cloth and fine twill both require about 8 taels. The goods from the Yuanfang Jiao firm have been falling sharply because sales have been sluggish. Yuan Yu silk has fallen by 1 to 2 taels, and Yuan Xi satin and others are down by 4 to 5 fen per yard, but the extreme tightness of credit is also a major reason.

Demand for Low-Grade Woolen Cloth Extremely High

The woolen cloth market was relatively stable yesterday. Traders from Xiamen and Sichuan continued to arrive, and there was an extraordinary shortage of lower-grade checkered twill and flower-patterned low-grade woolen cloth on the market. As a result, prices were very firm, as local merchants continued to search for supplies, with demand exceeding supply. The market sentiment in the guild was quite firm. The wholesale price of ordinary low-grade woolen cloth was universally quoted at 1 tael and 2 qian and a half, printed cloth at 1 tael and 5 qian, and No. 1 goods at 2 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen, but it was still difficult to obtain more. Because the inventory in Shanghai is not large, there is a trend of exhaustion and stockouts.
