Local News

Ma Zhanshan Does Not Fail the Nation

▲ Whose Responsibility is it that the Isolated Army has No Support?

Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, with an isolated army from a border province, resisted the stubborn Japanese invaders and supported them for half a month, but eventually withdrew from Heihe due to exhausted ammunition and no reinforcements. Alas, how sad!

▲ Guangdong Representatives Telegraph Guangdong for Assistance to Heihe Yesterday

▲ Telegram Already Sent Out Last Night

The three Guangdong representatives staying in Shanghai, Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaoshu, and Zou Haibin, believe that Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang Province, with a small force, resisted the violent Japanese, preserved the territory, and fought for national glory. His loyalty and courage are remarkable. However, an isolated army in a remote area cannot be sustained for long. At this critical juncture, it is necessary to provide strong practical assistance as soon as possible to reverse the precarious situation. If we continue to disregard and fail to help, standing idly by, we will not only fail Ma Zhanshan, but also fail to protect our territory. Therefore, they held a meeting at Wu's residence on Mercy Road at 5 p.m. yesterday and decided to jointly telegraph the Guangdong government, requesting them to assist Ma Zhanshan, the Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, as soon as possible. The telegram was drafted and sent out last night.

▲ Zhang Fakui Resolved to Await Orders to Depart

▲ The Chairman Does Not Deem His Intestinal Illness Worthy of Concern

Zhang Fakui, commander of the Fourth Army of the National Revolutionary Army, after telegraphing last time requesting to go to aid Ma Zhanshan and fight to the death with Japan, is now quietly waiting for a reply before departing. According to Zhang, there is a way to go to aid Heilongjiang, and he is eager to go. The doctors place great importance on his intestinal illness, which is still being treated, but he considers it insignificant. As the nation is in such a state, personal life and death are not worth considering.

Telegram from the Postal Workers' Volunteer Army

▲Request to the government for the issuance of firearms

▲Regularly held grand maneuvers

Since the establishment of the Shanghai Postal Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps, nearly two months have passed, and more than a thousand postal workers have volunteered to join. Over 700 have been incorporated into the ranks, forming a large corps with Mr. Zhang Kechang as the commander. Military uniforms and all equipment are very complete. They go to the north and south of the city for daily training, and the results are quite impressive. The corps has scheduled a grand maneuver on the 22nd of this month at 2:00 PM at the Qingyun Road open space in Zhabei. In addition to the participation of all the volunteers, there are also 30 members of the women's rescue team organized by the corps, 60 Boy Scouts, and 30 band members joining at the same time. Recently, moved by General Ma Zhanshan's lone army fighting the enemy, showing great loyalty and bravery, and filled with righteous indignation against the stubbornness of the Japanese, the corps specially telegraphed the National Government yesterday to volunteer to fight the Japanese and requested the issuance of firearms to the corps. It also telegraphed the Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, Ma Zhanshan, expressing condolences and a willingness to live and die together. The wording was particularly tragic. The two telegrams are recorded separately as follows:

To the National Government, Nanjing: Since the violent Japanese invaded us, the whole country has been united in hatred. The officials in the Northeast retreated without a fight, and Liaoning and Jilin were occupied. Now Heilongjiang Province is also in danger. Fortunately, our Chairman Ma is loyal and brave in defending the territory, repeatedly defeating strong enemies with a small force. However, the enemy is now launching a full-scale nationwide offensive against us. If we do not rise up to resist immediately, the borders will surely collapse, and our people will die without a trace. To not fight and await death is the government's crime; to fight and lose the country is the nation's responsibility. Time is critical! Our corps, upholding the principle of jointly resisting national humiliation, is willing to take up arms on the battlefield and live and die together with the generals and soldiers at the front. We earnestly implore your government to issue firearms as soon as possible so that we may await orders to be conscripted. The country will be fortunate; the nation will be fortunate. Respectfully, the Shanghai Postal Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps.

To Chairman Ma, Heilongjiang: To General Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang, and forwarded to all the loyal and brave generals and soldiers at the front. As the violent Japanese invade, the whole country shares a common hatred. However, the officials in the Northeast, fearing Japan by nature, retreated without a fight, causing our beautiful land to fall into the hands of foreign races. Fortunately, you, General, are loyal to the country, and the soldiers are brave, resisting Japan with a lone army and resolutely killing the enemy, bringing glory to the country and survival to the nation. As the news of victory spread, the whole country rejoiced. Our corps, upholding the principle of jointly resisting foreign aggression, immediately appealed to the government to issue firearms and volunteered to go to the front to live and die together with you, General, and all the soldiers. We respectfully report this and hope that you will continue your efforts, stand ready, and not allow the Japanese invaders to cross the Nen River and graze horses. Your loyalty and bravery will shine for thousands of years and endure with the sun and moon. Respectfully, the Shanghai Postal Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps.

▲Southeast Medical College

Rescue Team to Heilongjiang Departs

▲Departed north by train yesterday afternoon

▲More than 4,000 representatives saw them off　　▲People from all walks of life made donations

The rescue team of Southeast Medical College was originally scheduled to depart as a whole for Heilongjiang to rescue wounded soldiers on the front lines. Now, due to financial constraints, 30 advanced students departed by train at 3:15 PM yesterday. More than 400 representatives saw them off at the station, including all the teachers and students of the school and more than 4,000 representatives from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army of Jinan, Chih Tze, and Guanghua, as well as various labor unions. The details of the time are compiled as follows:

▲The entire team is organized into two sections: medical affairs and transportation affairs. The leader is Chen Chesheng, the commander is Zhang Gan (the one with the severed finger), and the deputy commander is Liu Changxin. However, the leader, Chen Chesheng, is the military instructor of the school and will escort them to Beiping. After the liaison with the Deputy Commander's office is completed, he will return south.

▲Departure situation The team first gathered at the old site of the Songhu Station, then formed a team and entered the No. 2 station. After the whole team entered the carriages, the commander Zhang Gan gave a speech thanking the representatives who came to see them off. At this time, the representatives shook hands with the team members to say goodbye, and some even shed tears. The tragic and righteous courage of the entire team was admirable. Not long after, the whistle sounded, and the representatives threw colorful confetti. In the tragic and enthusiastic slogans of "Down with Japanese Imperialism," the train headed west.

▲Zhang Gan's speech Representatives, today we are departing, and we are unworthy of your sending us off. I hope that after you return, you will continue your efforts and continue to go to the front line to fight the Japanese to the death. At the same time, we are extremely grateful to the staff of the Railway Bureau for donating the transportation costs for the entire team.

▲Team members' attire All team members wore gray military uniforms, carried backpacks weighing 20 kilograms, containing cotton-padded clothes, and a rescue bag embroidered with a red cross was hung on the left, fully loaded with medicines. A dahlia was inserted in the right pocket, colorful and magnificent. The vanguard was led by a large military flag of the Southeast Medical College Rescue Team with a red cross.

▲A glimpse of donations This time, various circles donated a lot of goods and money to the team going north, including more than 300 yuan donated by all the teachers and students of the school, ten boxes of rescue medicines, cotton wool, and bandages donated by Wuzhou Chinese and Western Medicine Store, and 36 jin of backpacks donated by Minli Middle School. Railway colleagues donated the travel expenses for all team members to Beijing. Various labor unions also donated a lot of biscuits.

▲Donations after the Incident in Heilongjiang

Living Weekly Society

Announces Method of Handling Donations

No Loss of Donations Diligently Collected

The Living Weekly Society, in response to the enthusiastic donations from comrades from all walks of life to support Heilongjiang, has received a large amount of money. In addition to the 53,407 yuan that has been remitted to the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, it received another 11,496 yuan and 96 cents yesterday, which has not yet been remitted. Because the military situation at the front is changing rapidly, and many enthusiastic comrades are concerned about this matter, the society solemnly announces several points as follows: (1) All donations are remitted daily to the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, telegraphed to Harbin, and transferred to General Ma. If General Ma has properly received the money, a receipt will be delivered in the future. If it cannot be delivered, it should be returned according to the bank's practice. (2) Whether the society will continue to remit and collect donations will depend on whether General Ma can still hold on and whether the money can be remitted. (3) If, due to the pressure of the situation, it is impossible to remit by telegraph, the collection of donations will have to be temporarily suspended. The unremitted and returned funds will be kept in a special account in a reliable bank and will be publicly and fairly disposed of in the most appropriate way, either by returning them to the original donors or by waiting for a second Ma Zhanshan to be supported, all in accordance with the donors' wishes. However, all of this must depend on the situation thereafter and will be announced later. In short, there will be no loss of the money that enthusiastic comrades have worked so hard to collect.

Seventy-Eighth Division Arrives in Shanghai

▲Stationed in Longhua and Zhabei, etc.

▲Another batch is expected to arrive today

The Seventy-Eighth Division of the Nineteenth Route Army, ordered to be stationed in Songhu, arrived in Shanghai on the Jiangyu轮 of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company at 1:30 PM yesterday. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Number of People Arriving This time, the Jiangyu transported the entire 156th Brigade, totaling two regiments, and a special service battalion of the division headquarters, a signal team, and all the officers of the division headquarters, totaling over 4,000 officers and soldiers, and dozens of warhorses.

▲Arrival Situation Before the ship arrived at the port, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters agreed that it would land at the Gaochangmiao Naval Wharf. Therefore, yesterday morning, Battalion Commander Ye of the Naval Guard Battalion designated it to dock at the wharf in front of the old dock of the shipyard and sent soldiers to take care of the wharf and prepare tea. After the ship docked there at 1:30 PM yesterday, several soldiers disembarked and were on guard near the wharf. All the officers and soldiers did not disembark and waited for orders.

▲Distribution of Defense The defense locations after the division arrived in Shanghai have been determined. The Second Regiment of the 156th Brigade will be stationed in Longhua, the old site of the former Tax Police Regiment Headquarters. It is said that the division headquarters will be located in the Garrison Headquarters. The Fourth Regiment will take the train from the South Station to Zhabei to take charge of the Zhabei garrison. It is said that the brigade headquarters will be located in a certain guild hall in Zhabei, with Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan stationed there.

▲Continuing Arrival Today The First and Fifth Regiments of the division will arrive in Shanghai on the Jiangtian轮 from Xun. It is expected that they will arrive in Shanghai at noon tomorrow and will be responsible for the defense of the Wusong River Bay area.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Designated

Xinming Goes to Japan to Carry Overseas Chinese

▲Departing around the end of the month

▲Decided to send a ship The Ministry of Communications sent a telegram to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ordering it to send a ship to Japan to transport overseas Chinese back to China. The company initially planned to send the Xinfeng轮 to Yokohama. However, the Xinfeng is currently under repair and only entered the inner river machinery factory yesterday and started work. It will take some time to repair and leave the factory. The business department changed its plan and sent the Xinming轮 to Japan. Now, the Xinming轮 just left Shanghai for Tianjin the day before and must wait for it to return to Shanghai before it can cross to the east. It is expected to depart on the 29th or 30th of this month. It was agreed with Director Guo yesterday and telegraphed to the consulate in Yokohama to inform the overseas Chinese to wait and also telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to prepare the ship's license and other items to be obtained when leaving the port.

▲Preparing Procedures Before a Chinese ship goes to Japan, the preparations for the pilot, ship's license, and wharf must be completed first to avoid temporary obstacles. It was decided by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday that all matters related to the Xinming轮's voyage to the east should be prepared by the Ministry to make it simpler. Now, there are still more than ten days before the ship departs, so the company specially telegraphed the Ministry to order the consul stationed in Yokohama to contact the Japanese side in advance regarding import and export and ship docking matters for convenience.

Yangtze River Japanese Warships

Obstruct Passage of Chinese Ships

▲Obstructing the Zhenjiang River

▲Navigation Route is Blocked

▲Four Warships Block the River Yesterday, the various shipping companies in this port received an urgent telegram from Zhenjiang, stating that four Japanese warships stationed in Zhenjiang have been blocking the river recently, obstructing our navigation route. The navigation of ships going up and down the river is very difficult. A little carelessness can lead to contact. This not only hinders the navigation route but also endangers the safety of the ships. It is feared that it will cause other disputes, which is a hidden danger for international trade and transportation. It is recommended that the Japanese warships be ordered to move to a safe area to avoid causing trouble.

▲Letter Requesting the Customs Service to Move the Ships The various shipping companies who received the telegram were unanimous that Zhenjiang is a must-pass place for river boats, and the river surface is our national territory. Now is the low water season of the Yangtze River. If the navigation route is blocked, it is more likely to cause danger. They decided to send a public letter to the Inspector General of Customs requesting him to inform the Zhenjiang Customs Service as soon as possible to order the four Japanese warships stationed in Zhenjiang to move to a safe location that does not obstruct the navigation route, so that traffic is not hindered and ships can be secured. This letter was sent out yesterday.

Wu Chaoshu Talks About

The Nine-Power Treaty and the League of Nations Covenant

▲If Our Country Relies Entirely on Others

▲Then All Three Agreements Are Not Applicable

According to the American policy reported by the Paris Telegram Agency, the most important thing is the Washington Nine-Power Treaty and the Open Door Policy in the three northeastern provinces. The attitude of the United States towards resolving the Manchurian issue seems to be appropriate to invoke the Nine-Power Treaty, and many enemies in our country also believe that invoking the Nine-Power Treaty is better than invoking the League of Nations Covenant. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency specially visited Dr. Wu Chaoshu at his private residence at 10:45 AM yesterday. According to the conversation, the League of Nations Covenant, the Paris Peace Pact, and the Washington Nine-Power Treaty are all applicable or not applicable to the resolution of the three northeastern provinces' problems. I believe that if our country does not rely on itself and relies entirely on others, then all three agreements are not applicable. This is just like what I said yesterday, that is, we should be good at invoking them. As for whether the Article 11 of the Covenant (the reporter's note: This article stipulates that when any member country experiences any war or a similar threat of war, the League should take appropriate and effective measures to maintain peace among the countries, and any member country of the League may request the Assembly or the Council to pay attention to it) cited by our country's representative in the League of Nations to resolve the three northeastern provinces' problems is appropriate, or should be based on Article 16 (This article stipulates that if a member country of the League disregards the provisions of this chapter and does not submit the dispute to arbitration or legal resolution, nor submits it to the League for resolution, or engages in war within three months after submitting it for resolution, it shall be considered an act of war against all member countries of the League. Other member countries shall immediately impose commercial and financial sanctions on this defaulting country. When necessary, the member countries shall jointly send troops to achieve the purpose of protecting the League Covenant.) to request it to be more powerful, in fact, the League of Nations Covenant, not only Article 11 and Article 16 can be cited, but at least there are two or three more articles that can be proposed. However, whether Article 11, which our country is citing now, is the best is still a question. Article 16 should be studied in detail before it can be used. Furthermore, if our country asks the countries that signed the Nine-Power Treaty to discuss this matter, whether the treaty has sanctions provisions such as Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, then the treaty text can be examined to find out.

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement Reported Yesterday

▲Minutes of the Executive Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association: The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held its fourteenth executive committee meeting at 4 PM yesterday, with over forty executive committee members present. Lu Jingshi and Chu Huiseng chaired the meeting, and Zhao Shusheng and Tong Yikang served as recorders. The following cases were discussed: (1) The Design Committee submitted a proposed plan for handling confiscated Japanese goods for approval. It was resolved to postpone the decision until a survey and statistics on the confiscated Japanese goods are completed. (2) Committee member Wang Changyuan raised the issue that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce implemented the "Measures for Handling Confiscated Japanese Goods in the City," decided by the Committee for Economic Severance of Relations with Japan, without obtaining the approval of this meeting, and immediately published it in the newspapers, affecting the work of this association. It was resolved (A) to send a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce stating that all actions and resolutions of the committee must be decided by this association and must not be disposed of without authorization; (B) to publish an announcement in the newspaper stating that the measures for handling confiscated Japanese goods will be formulated after the survey and statistics are completed, and that the "Measures for Handling Confiscated Japanese Goods" published in the newspapers by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce on the previous day without the approval of this meeting will not take effect. (3) Committee members Yu Hualong and others raised the issue regarding Chen Yuansong's protection of unscrupulous merchants, which had been previously referred for review. The review has now been completed, and a report has been prepared for discussion. It was resolved to publish the review report and send a letter to Committee member Chen requesting him to continue working with the association. (4) Committee members Chu Huiseng, Wang Hanliang, and Li Yongxiang raised the issue of staff members of the association disobeying the orders of the standing committee, which had been previously referred for review. The review has now been completed, and a report has been prepared for discussion. It was resolved to record a major demerit against staff member Jiang Menggu as a warning. This association should petition the National Government to implement economic sanctions and sever diplomatic relations, and, based on Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, request the member states of the League to sever economic relations with Japan together, and request the National Government to take over the lost territories by force. The standing committee resolved to refer the matter to the general meeting for public resolution, which was approved. ▲Review Report on the Chen Yuansong Case: On October 23rd, the 20th year of the Republic of China, this association received an official letter, along with five original documents, instructing the undersigned to review the reports from the investigation, inspection, and reconnaissance departments regarding Chen Yuansong's protection of unscrupulous merchants and Chen Yuansong's report of being beaten and detained. The review results, excluding the report from the investigation department, which is not within the scope of the review, are divided into two parts as follows: (1) Chen Yuansong did not protect unscrupulous merchants. The investigation revealed that the case originated from repeated reports from the inspection department stating that Xie Da Xiang, Bao Da Xiang, Yuan Chang Xiang, and Xin Da Xiang shops privately purchased a large number of Japanese goods from Japanese merchants. On the morning of October 17th, the department assigned Ge Yunting and others to go to investigate with the investigation department and Nanshi inspectors, resulting in a dispute and the tragic arrest of three staff members at 11:45 AM. As for Chen Yuansong rushing to the scene, it was after 3:00 PM, and he had first gone to this association to inquire about the facts from the two standing committee members, Wang and Fang. Therefore, Chen Yuansong's rushing to explain was to ease the dispute between the two parties in the capacity of the chairman of the Cotton Cloth Industry Association, and there was no intention to protect unscrupulous merchants. Furthermore, judging from the words in the reports after Chen Yuansong and the inspection department met, the biggest disagreement was that the action of the inspection department did not comply with this association's announcement on October 10th and the resolution to inspect Japanese goods with various trade associations. Therefore, Chen Yuansong's rushing to explain was to exercise the functions of his trade association based on the resolution of this association, and not to protect unscrupulous merchants. As for the inspection of Japanese goods by the inspection department, it must be determined whether it violates the resolution. (2) The part about Chen Yuansong being beaten and detained: Regarding Chen Yuansong being beaten and detained, there is no description of Chen Yuansong being beaten in the reports of the inspection and reconnaissance departments. In Chen Yuansong's report, there is a statement that Jiang Menggu took the lead in gathering people to beat him fiercely, which is further proved by the fact that Chen Yuansong and others were injured, and in the reconnaissance department's report, "Executive Committee member Zheng Chengqing stated that Chen Yuansong was not allowed to make any kind of statement in the inspection department. If he leaves the inspection department, he is unwilling to take responsibility," etc. Therefore, there is no doubt that Chen Yuansong was indeed beaten. As for the detention of Chen Yuansong, according to the report of the inspection department, it was because Chen Yuansong's bodyguard suddenly showed a gun to demonstrate. The reconnaissance personnel saw that the situation was not good and were afraid of causing a major disaster, so they put Chen, Ke, and the bodyguard into the side room to take temporary refuge, otherwise the consequences would be even more unimaginable, etc., which is different from the details stated in the reconnaissance report that the department temporarily detained Chen Yuansong and others to wait for a solution, but the bodyguard Mao Lianke showed his gun and wanted to fire, and it is also different from Chen Yuansong's report that he was beaten and then detained, tied with ropes, and treated as a bandit. Proved by the fact that after the incident, the staff repeatedly violated the orders of the standing committee and refused to release him, and falsely reported the next day that Chen Yuansong and others were robbed and that all staff members held a meeting to strike, the staff of this association at all levels abused their power to beat and detain people and violated the orders of the standing committee. However, based on the above facts, the staff members' actions were excessive due to temporary indignation and should be held accountable, but they should also be understood for being motivated by patriotic enthusiasm. November 10th, the 20th year of the Republic of China, review committee members Hu Fengxiang, Hu Shuhua, Yu Hualong, Tao Baichuan, and Chen Tingrui. The original was signed by Hu Fengxiang, Yu Hualong, and Chen Tingrui.

Silk Rayon Weaving Trade Association

Explains the Process of Changing to Run a Sizing Factory

▲Sends Letters to Wuxi, Wujin, and Other Associations to Clear Up Misunderstandings

Since the invasion of Northeast China by the violent Japanese and the nationwide implementation of the economic boycott against Japan, the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association once sent a letter to the Silk Rayon Weaving Trade Association, instructing it to change the more than 60,000 yuan of cotton industry yarn factory shares previously collected to run a cotton industry sizing factory. The association then convened a meeting of initiators to actively prepare and sent letters to trade associations in various places to solicit shares. However, the dyeing and weaving trade associations in Jiangyin, Wujin, Wuxi, and other places had previously made a resolution when soliciting initiators for the cotton industry yarn factory that "the share money shall not be used for other purposes if the yarn factory is not established." Now that the cotton industry yarn factory has not yet been established, but the share money is suddenly changed to run a sizing factory, it is in conflict with the previous resolution, so they have sent letters expressing their opposition and refusing to join. The Silk Rayon Weaving Trade Association believes that changing the cotton industry yarn factory shares to run a sizing factory is due to the letter from the Anti-Japanese Association and is not the association's own proposal, and that opening a sizing factory is also an important task for saving cotton weaving raw materials. It cannot stop preparing due to the opposition of one or two trade associations. Therefore, yesterday, it specially sent letters to the trade associations in Jiangyin, Wujin, Wuxi, and other places to explain the process and methods, so as to clear up misunderstandings and encourage active share subscriptions, so as to unite and make the cotton industry sizing factory a reality as soon as possible.

China Merchants Bureau Expands Shipping Industry

▲Orders Two Cargo Ships to Run Exclusively on the Yangtze River

▲Additionally, Two Oil Tankers Will Sail to the South Seas

Since Guo Waifeng, a special commissioner of the China Merchants Bureau, took office, he has strived to rectify and develop state-owned shipping affairs. Currently, because the original 25 merchant ships sailing on the Yangtze River, South Seas, North Seas, and other routes are sometimes insufficient, he recently ordered two new-style double-leaf diesel cargo ships from the Shanghai Da Zhonghua Shipbuilding and Machinery Factory. The contract has been signed for a period of six months. The ship is 186 feet long, 32 feet wide, 11 feet 6 inches deep, has a draft of 9 feet, and a speed of 10 nautical miles per hour. It is expected to be completed by May of next year and will be used exclusively for transporting goods on the Yangtze River in the future. He also purchased two new-style ocean-going vessels from a Norwegian shipping company. The contract has been signed. The ship names are BESTIC BESTUIR, with a weight of 2,878 tons, a length of 251 feet, a depth of 20 feet 3 inches, a draft of 17 feet 9 inches, and a speed of 9 to 10 nautical miles per hour. They were built in 1918. The two ships have already set sail from Norway to China, and one of them is expected to arrive next week and will be used exclusively for the South Seas route (sailing from Shanghai to Guangzhou, passing through Shantou, Xiamen, Hong Kong, and other ports along the way).

You Bolu Case: Private Prosecution Withdrawn

▲Postal Workers Union Requests Instructions

▲City Executive Committee Explains According to Law

Guomin News Agency reports that the City Executive Committee previously received a report from the Shanghai Postal Workers Union regarding the families of the dead and injured in the You Bolu shooting of civilians case, requesting clear instructions on whether to withdraw the private prosecution and the right to independent prosecution in order to clarify doubts. It is heard that the City Executive Committee has clearly explained it according to the law. The original reply is recorded as follows: "The report is noted. This association's consultation with the municipal government to provide compensation to the family members is purely out of the family members' request, as the report says, 'with compassion,' which is an obligation. As for the attached private prosecution part, because the public prosecution and the private prosecution are the rights of claim arising from the same criminal facts, and are heard and judged in the same criminal trial. However, the purpose of the public prosecution is to prove the crime and apply the penalty, with national power as the main focus, and the principle of exercising authority, that is, the principle of intervention. The purpose of the private prosecution is to compensate for the damage caused by the crime, with the victim as the main focus, and the principle of exercising the right of disposal, that is, the principle of non-intervention. Therefore, whether to file a private prosecution, or whether to withdraw it after it has been filed, is up to the parties' intention and does not affect the public prosecution. According to Article 507 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the liability for compensation in civil actions incidental to criminal proceedings shall be determined in accordance with the Civil Code. Furthermore, according to Article 306 of the Civil Procedure Regulations, the plaintiff may withdraw all or part of the lawsuit before the judgment becomes final. Therefore, the private prosecution that has already been settled can naturally be withdrawn according to law, and the public prosecution will still proceed as usual." This is the reply.

Death of a Japanese Ronin

▲Impersonates a Chinese to Recruit a Prostitute for Company

▲Pawns Clothes to Pay for the Night

▲Only After Suicide Is It Known to Be a Japanese

The Japanese ronin, Ota Ryohei, was 29 years old this year and worked as a sailor on a ship, traveling between China and Japan from time to time. He spoke extremely fluent Ningbo dialect. He had no address in Shanghai. On the 15th of this month, he alone, using a Chinese name, changed his name to Yu Liren, 26 years old, from Ningbo, to a hotel opened by a Chinese at 491 Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, to rent a room to stay in. That night, he recruited a Chinese prostitute, Wang Asi, from Changshu, to spend the night with him. The next day, because he had no money, he ordered the tea boy to pawn his clothes for three yuan to pay the prostitute for the night. Then he asked for one yuan back for other uses and agreed that the prostitute would come again on the afternoon of the 18th. It is not known why the Japanese was stimulated and suddenly had the idea of ​​being tired of the world. On the evening of the 17th, he committed suicide by taking poison. It was not until 3 PM on the 18th that the prostitute Wang Asi went to the hotel again and ordered the tea boy to open the door and enter the room. He did not respond when called. Seeing him lying stiffly on the bed, he was already dead when touched. The hotel reported it to the police, who sent detectives to investigate, still thinking that he was Chinese. A medicine bottle was copied from under the bed and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for autopsy. Because no relatives could be found, they went to the hotel room again to check carefully. Three suicide notes were found in the bedding on the bed. One to the hotel, instructing them to notify Yu Linfa (fabricated), a relative of the family outside Ximen, Cixi, Ningbo. One to the Japanese consulate, and one to his friend Hyodo Eizan at 9 Sanyi Lane, North Sichuan Road. They immediately went to notify them and reported it to the Second Special Court to send personnel for inspection. When Prosecutor Lou Guangguang arrived at the morgue at 10 AM yesterday with forensic doctor Wei Ligong and clerk Zhao Yifen, the Japanese consulate had sent staff member Yamaji Yoshio and the corpse friend Hyodo Eizan to the place to identify the corpse and request to take it back for burial. After the prosecutor and forensic doctor verified that the deceased had indeed committed suicide by taking poison before his death, they questioned the tea boy and the prostitute about the circumstances of the discovery. The official instructed that the body be allowed to be claimed back for burial by the corpse friend Hyodo Eizan after he made a guarantee. Then the corpse friend brought the coffin to the morgue, and another Japanese man wiped the whole body of the corpse with potion before putting it in the coffin and carrying it to Zhabei for burial.

National Products

The Calcium Carbonate Raw Material Factory ships to the Greater China Rubber Factory. It is an independently funded establishment, managed by Xue Fuji, Wu Zhesheng, Yu Xingben, and others, who have studied in Japan for many years and have a deep understanding of industry. Since the establishment of the factory in 1928, its products have been perfect, winning unparalleled praise in the domestic market. The factory produces more than 20,000 pairs of Double Coin brand galoshes and athletic shoes for men and women daily, making it the largest rubber factory in China. In recent years, recognizing the lack of domestic manufacturing of raw materials, which relied on imports, and believing that this was not a fundamental way to promote national products, the factory prepared to build its own Greater China Calcium (i.e., basic industrial raw material calcium carbonate) Factory in the Xujiahui Road area of southern Shanghai last autumn. Mr. Zhu Huiren, manager and technician of the raw material factory, was commissioned to use the latest method, using machinery to refine carbon dioxide gas into calcium carbonate. Shipments began in mid-October. The quality is excellent, surpassing imports. It is reported that the factory's annual output is estimated at about four tons per day, just enough for its own use. It is expected that there will be a large output starting in January next year to supply the national products industry. This is truly good news for the national products raw material industry.

▲Another Creditors' Meeting Established

Justice Bank, located at 452 Jiangxi Road in this city, suddenly closed its doors on November 19, announcing the suspension of payments. Shanghai Justice Bank suddenly suspended business yesterday (November 19). The bank's creditors held a creditors' meeting at 11:00 am yesterday at the Yan Luqing Law Firm, Room 1, No. 9 Edward Road. Lawyer Yan was elected as chairman and Mr. Zhu Yunxian as secretary. The meeting was formally convened and various important cases were discussed for a long time until the meeting adjourned at 12:30 pm. The resolutions are recorded below: (1) The association is named the Justice Bank Creditors' Association; (2) The association will temporarily borrow the Zhou Xiangtai Redwood Furniture Store at 214 Dongjie Street, inside Dadongmen, for office space; (3) Creditors who have not joined the association will be allowed to continue to join and register without paying a registration fee; (4) The association will hire Lawyer Yan as the agent lawyer; (5) Obtain the balance sheet of Justice Bank as of the date of the suspension of business; (6) Entrust Lawyer Yan to pursue legal action to achieve the goal of fully recovering deposits.

Regulations for Transporting Livestock Licensing

▲Announced by the Municipal Health Bureau

The Municipal Health Bureau issued a notice yesterday, saying: In order to prevent the slaughter and sale of livestock with epidemic diseases and to emphasize public health, the bureau previously stipulated that livestock must be transported with separate licenses for inspection. Now, it has been revised. All healthy live livestock transported only within the municipality's directly governed districts do not need to apply for a license and are allowed to be transported freely. However, those transported from the directly governed districts, passing through the concessions, and still arriving at the directly governed districts (such as from Nanshi to Zhabei) still need to apply for a special license. In addition, livestock transported from the directly governed districts to the concessions for shipment outside the city should still use an export license. Livestock transported to the concessions still need to be inspected before slaughter and apply for an inspection form, as in the past. This has been submitted to the municipal government for approval. The revised regulations for the transport of livestock licensing are hereby announced for public knowledge. This notice.

Apprentice Accused of Arson

▲Because of Stealing Silver Dollars and Being Dismissed

▲Harboring Resentment and Committing This Heinous Act

Chen Daying, a 16-year-old apprentice from Haiyan at Wan Shen Soy Sauce Garden, No. 857-858 Zhoujiazui Road, after closing the shop at around 10 pm the night before, personally took a large pile of salt wrapping paper in the shop, soaked it with kerosene, placed it under the counter, and lit it on fire. In an instant, thick smoke filled the area, almost causing a fire. Yang Liunian, a fellow apprentice upstairs, noticed it, immediately went downstairs and shouted, and the shop owner Feng Fusong and others managed to put out the fire, fortunately preventing a disaster. The nearby fire brigade also arrived with their fire truck to put out the fire, but it was already extinguished. Detective Li Hongsheng arrested the apprentice Chen and detained him in the Huishan Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the case, and said that the police charged the defendant with arson under Article 187, Section 1 of the Criminal Law. The investigation revealed that the defendant had previously stolen silver dollars and was discovered by the shop owner, who wanted to dismiss him, leading to this disaster to vent his anger. Now, considering his young age and ignorance, he asked for leniency. According to shop owner Feng Fusong's statement, the defendant had been an apprentice in his shop for more than two years. In July of this year, ten silver dollars were lost in the shop. It was discovered that he had stolen them, and he was planning to dismiss him. He learned of this and committed this heinous act. According to the testimony of a fellow apprentice in the shop, Yang Liunian: "I sleep with the defendant every night in the pavilion upstairs. Last night, I saw him watering the paper with kerosene and setting the fire." According to shop assistant Xu Jimei's testimony, "The shop's rules are that after closing the shop every night, the defendant turns off the lights before going upstairs to bed, but this happened after I went upstairs." According to the woman Feng Jinshi, the shop owner's sister-in-law, who lived in the front building, "I heard Yang Liunian shouting that there was a fire, I ran downstairs in surprise and helped put it out. When I questioned the defendant, he firmly denied that he set the fire. I don't know anything about stealing silver dollars or being dismissed. Moreover, when the fire broke out, I had already gone upstairs and taken off my clothes, wanting to sleep, not in the shop." After reviewing the confession, Judge Shen Bingrong instructed the lawyer to defend the defendant once, and ordered him to be remanded in custody for sentencing on a scheduled date.

Beggar Dies from Gluttony

Beggar Wang Zhishan, from Ningbo, 48 years old, specializes in picking up cigarette butts and selling old items on the street to make a living. Yesterday afternoon at around 5 pm, Wang was picking up discarded items in a pile of garbage in the area of ​​Zilaihuo Street in the French Concession. He suddenly discovered a pile of fish entrails, and he was overjoyed. He took it back, cooked it, and ate it. Unexpectedly, he suddenly had severe abdominal pain in the evening, lay on the ground groaning. The fellow beggars were shocked and rushed him to Renji Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the poisoning was too deep, and he died on the way before reaching the hospital. The hospital notified the Dadazimingzhong Police Station, which sent police to carry the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch and reported it to the court for inspection.

Ye Zhongfang Accused of Trivial Matters

▲Plaintiff is Neighbor Zhou Shen Yunzhu

▲Accused of Obstructing Freedom and Damaging Property

Ye Zhongfang, nicknamed "Little Shaker," and tea servant Xu Are, were recently sued in the First Special District Court by Zhou Shen Yunzhu, wife of lawyer Zhou Yanzuo, accusing Ye of obstructing freedom and damaging property. It is said that the cause of this case is extremely minor, and the case is quite laughable. Here is an excerpt from the indictment: "For obstructing freedom and damaging buildings, I beg you to punish the matter. The defendant Ye Zhongfang is a cohabiting neighbor (residing at No. 12 Jing'an Temple Road). He is a young man without a job. Every night, he summons three or four prostitutes, making loud noises and revelry until dawn. The house is a writing room style. Room 21, where Ye lives, is directly opposite the three-story building where the plaintiff lives. The plaintiff and her son Shi Gong cannot sleep peacefully all night, and their spirits are very painful. Now the young child is sick because of this (omitted). I have reasoned with him, but I have been insulted and scolded. On the 8th of this month at 9:00 am, Ye moved from Room 18 to Room 21, and deliberately instructed the second defendant Xu Are to dismantle the upper and lower stairs of the three-story building, move them elsewhere, and destroy the handrails installed on the stairs, instead of walking through the corridor on the south side. By the afternoon of the next day, because Ye refused to reinstall them, I hired a carpenter to install them myself. For one night and a half day, the plaintiff could not go downstairs. Therefore, the defendant has committed the crime of obstructing freedom in violation of Article 316 of the Criminal Law and the crime of damaging the property of others in violation of Article 382." Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao Xiefei ascended the Fifth Criminal Court to hear the case. Ye Zhongfang and Xu Are arrived at the court around 2:00 pm and entrusted lawyer Jiang Baolian to defend them. The plaintiff Xu Yunzhu was represented by her husband, lawyer Zhou Yanzuo, and female lawyer Shi Liang. Zhou Shen Yunzhu filed a case and explained the previous situation, her words being similar to the indictment, and will not be repeated. Then, according to plaintiff witness Wang Quangen's statement, he used to be a clerk in Zhou Lawyer's office and is now selling bean paste candy at No. 46 Guangdong Road. On the morning of the 9th of this month, because a friend surnamed Luo wanted to hire Zhou Lawyer as a legal advisor, he went there, but there was no one in Zhou Lawyer's writing room. He also saw that the stairs up and down the three-story building where Zhou Lawyer lived were also gone. He did not know anything else. When questioned, Ye Zhongfang confessed that the plaintiff's claim that he summoned prostitutes every night and reveled all night was not true. Even if women came, they were either relatives or wives, how could they be referred to as prostitutes? As for reveling all night, wouldn't I myself want to sleep? The plaintiff also said that dismantling the stairs caused them to be unable to go up and down for one night and a half day. On the night of the 8th, because a friend wanted to lease my room, I moved the items in my room to the next room that night. However, because a ladder blocked the corridor outside the door, I temporarily dismantled it with the permission of the rental agent's office. After the matter was completed, I immediately reinstalled it. Moreover, the second defendant Xu Are also lived on the third floor and still went up to sleep that night. Since Xu could go upstairs, the plaintiff could of course go downstairs. When Xu Are was questioned, he confessed that the stairs were reinstalled that night. Finally, the lawyers for both parties began to debate. The plaintiff's lawyer said that the cause of this matter was extremely minor and there was no need to delve into it. If the defendants could admit their mistakes, the court could slightly warn them and the matter could be concluded. Otherwise, please make a judgment according to the law. The defendant's lawyer said that the plaintiff's accusations were not supported by sufficient evidence and should be dismissed. The defendant Ye Zhongfang denied his guilt in court and said that he still needed to file a counterclaim for false accusation. Judge Xiao reviewed the confession and announced that the debate in this case was over and sentencing was scheduled for the morning of the 25th.

Eagle Becomes Peacock

▲Wang Yunfang Accuses Yongxing Silver Shop

▲Without an Apology, a Small Matter Becomes a Lawsuit

Wang Yunfang, a famous actress on the Tianchan Stage, on September 25, ordered her servant Afu to wipe a silver tripod given by a friend with silver powder. Afu accidentally broke the eagle's leg on the lid. She then entrusted the silver object, along with the eagle's footrest, to her colleague Cui Wanshun to be repaired at Yongxing Silver Shop on Guangdong Road, saying it would take about a week. She stated that the repair fee was one yuan. At that time, she asked the silver shop for a receipt, but the shop clerk said that they were old customers of Wang Ling, and such a small item could be exempted from this procedure. Cui agreed, thinking that no accidents would occur. Unexpectedly, when he went to pick it up on time, the eagle had become a peacock and was no longer the original item. He immediately argued with them. The shop clerk firmly denied that there was any mistake in replacing the eagle with a peacock. Cui had to return and tell Wang Ling. She was shocked when she heard this and went to the silver shop to see it. It was indeed true. She immediately negotiated with them, asking them to check if there was a mistake in mislabeling. The shop clerks, etc., said that this was the original item and there was no mistake. Wang Ling thought that the small silver item was not of great value and asked the shop owner to admit their mistake and express their apology. She would not pursue the matter. But the shop clerks, etc., not only refused, but also spoke rudely and unreasonably, saying that they were not afraid to resolve this matter through law. Wang Ling was extremely angry and hired lawyer E Sen to accuse the silver shop owner of breach of trust in the First Special District Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong presided over the Third Criminal Court to summon them. According to the plaintiff Wang Yunfang, she explained the previous situation. When questioned, the manager of Yongxing Silver Shop, Zhang, confessed that the shop owner had important matters and had already left Shanghai. Because he was not in the shop at the time, this incident occurred. However, according to the shop clerks, it was the original item, which caused the loss of the old customer's feelings. Please forgive me. Judge Shen persuaded both parties and ordered Yongxing Silver Shop to return the original eagle or apologize to the plaintiff. He then ordered the case to be withdrawn.

Coal Freight Case

Railway Department's Telegram to the City Chamber of Commerce Yesterday

▲Detailed Account of the Consultation Process Regarding This Case

The City Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Railway Department yesterday regarding the coal transportation case on the Jiaoji Railway, detailing the process. The original telegram is as follows: Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Shanghai Coal Industry Association, China National Coal Production and Sales Association: Regarding the special price for coal transportation on the Jiaoji Railway, previously, this association, etc., forwarded telegrams from coal merchants stating the urgency of coal shortage in Shanghai and the need for coal from Shandong to alleviate the situation, requesting temporary cancellation to the Ministry. The Ministry has already responded accordingly. Subsequently, the Ministry also considered the coal shortage in various regions and the urgent need for relief, planning to temporarily suspend the coal transportation price increase for three months. However, since Shandong coal has always been primarily exported, accounting for the majority, this time, with the aim of alleviating the domestic coal shortage, all Shandong coal must be transported to Shanghai to alleviate the situation. Only in this way can all sectors of the country using coal enjoy the benefit of reduced freight rates, and the coal shortage will not materialize. Furthermore, with the reduction in freight rates, the railway and mines have a mutual obligation to support each other, and the coal merchants should also supply railway coal at a low price, according to the established practices of various railways. Therefore, after the representatives requested a postponement of the price increase for several months, the following three proposals were made to the coal merchants: (1) Shandong Province should make every effort to transport coal to Shanghai, exclusively for domestic use; (2) During this time of national crisis, coal prices must not be increased; (3) Coal for the Jiaoji Railway should be supplied at a low price as before. These three measures are the fairest and essential for alleviating the domestic coal shortage. The representatives have fully committed to the first two proposals, and expressed that they are willing to comply with the third proposal after consultation with the railway authorities. They also stated that they have telegraphed to advise against work stoppages. Unexpectedly, two days after the representatives agreed to the telegram, the work stoppage still occurred on November 1st. Later, the Shandong Zibo Zhangwei Coal Mining Industry Association submitted a report stating that regarding the above three proposals, only the second proposal was the same. As for the third proposal, when the Ministry initially requested that railway coal be supplied at the original price, the representatives changed it to only acknowledging a low price, without specifying the extent of the low price. Furthermore, they added appendices such as canceling the price increase and agreeing on fairness, with the aim of fundamentally overturning the agreed-upon plan. It is unclear whether the merchants, having sent representatives, are aware that the commitments made by the representatives are equivalent to the merchants' own commitments and cannot be changed. As for the first proposal, it is necessary to exclude mines that have existing contracts and are permitted to be developed with foreign investment by the government. It is found that most of the coal mines along the Jiaoji Railway are jointly operated with Japanese investment, and the coal produced is also transported to Japan. Only a small amount is usually transported to Shanghai. Now, if price increases are prohibited, it is inevitable that coal will still be transported to Japan for profit-making purposes. This time, the Ministry is reducing freight rates to alleviate the coal shortage, and coal mining merchants should also transport all their products to Shanghai or other parts of the country to alleviate the coal shortage. Now, the coal mining representatives declare that the complete alleviation of the coal shortage in Shanghai, which they promised, must exclude mines that have existing contracts and are invested in by foreigners. How much coal can be transported to Shanghai to alleviate the situation then? It seems that when coal mining merchants request reduced freight rates, they send out telegrams and appeals, using the domestic coal shortage as an excuse, implying that the bankruptcy of the national industry depends on whether Shandong coal can be transported to Shanghai. The inability to transport Shandong coal to Shanghai is attributed to the Jiaoji price increase of twenty cents. However, the result is that they are not at all concerned about the domestic coal shortage, but rather want to supply cheap coal to Japanese users, with the coal merchants profiting from it. The Association's current request for reduced freight rates is also intended to alleviate the coal shortage. Although the special price is planned to be temporarily suspended, if the coal merchants along the Jiaoji Railway do not alleviate the domestic shortage but instead alleviate the Japanese needs, this is probably not what the Association desires either. The Ministry, in addition to already rejecting the Shandong Zibo Zhangwei Coal Mining Industry Association's report for discrepancies with the representatives' promises, should instruct the Association on how to correct this situation in order to thoroughly alleviate the domestic coal shortage. The circumstances of this case are telegraphed for your information. Furthermore, regarding the second item, that all coal in Shanghai should not be subject to price increases, according to the representatives, there is a resolution to this effect, which has been promulgated. However, there are rumors that coal prices are still inevitably rising. We hope that you will provide details on how this resolution is formulated and whether it has binding effect. Please reply as soon as possible. Railway Department, sealed by Xiao.

Party and Government Organs

Deadline for Datong Workers to Resume Work

▲Failure to Comply within Three Days Will Be Considered Voluntary Resignation

▲The Company Is Allowed to Recruit New Workers to Replenish the Workforce

▲City Chamber of Commerce Telegram Urges Swift Cessation

Following the strike by all employees of the Datong Bookstore's head office in this city, the Party and government organs jointly issued a public notice yesterday, setting a deadline of three days for resuming work. Failure to comply will be considered voluntary resignation, and the company is allowed to recruit new workers to replenish the workforce. Worker Xu Xinong has been arrested, and the labor union has scheduled an emergency meeting today to discuss countermeasures. The details of each item are recorded as follows: ▲Deadline for Resuming Work (1) (Public Notice) The Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs jointly issued a public notice yesterday, stating that the workers of the Datong Bookstore arbitrarily went on strike on the morning of the 16th of this month and organized a strike committee to preside over the matter. Disregarding the national crisis and disturbing public order, it is clear that they lack a basic sense of righteousness. The Committee and Bureau have already jointly issued a public notice, earnestly advising them to resume work first. However, they have dared to adopt a wait-and-see attitude and disregard the law until today. In view of the current national crisis and to maintain public order in this city, the Committee and Bureau are unable to condone this behavior. They hereby jointly issue a public notice, instructing all workers of the bookstore to resume work by a specified date and await mediation by the Committee and Bureau in accordance with the law. If they fail to resume work within three days, the bookstore will be allowed to treat their actions as voluntary resignation and recruit new workers to replenish the workforce. They must not make a mistake. It is imperative that they comply. (2) (Instruction) The Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs jointly issued an instruction to the Publishing Industry Labor Union yesterday, stating that the workers of the Datong Bookstore arbitrarily went on strike this time without prior application or subsequent reporting. At a time when the country is facing a crisis, this is an act of disturbing public order. Furthermore, they have organized a strike committee to preside over the matter, daring to disregard the law and willingly destroy industry. It is clear that they lack a basic sense of righteousness. The Committee and Bureau have already jointly issued a public notice, earnestly advising them to resume work. However, they are still waiting and watching until today. Considering the difficult times, the Committee and Bureau are unable to condone this behavior. In addition to issuing another joint public notice, the Committee urgently instructs the Labor Union to comply and immediately take responsibility for advising the workers of the bookstore to resume work uniformly within three days of receiving this document and await mediation by the Committee and Bureau in accordance with the law. If they fail to resume work within the deadline, the bookstore will be allowed to treat their actions as voluntary resignation and recruit new workers to replenish the workforce. Furthermore, they must be thoroughly informed to avoid delay or making a mistake. It is imperative that they comply.

▲City Chamber of Commerce Telegram The Shanghai Special Municipality Party Department, Municipal Government, and Bureau of Social Affairs: Considering that the country is facing a crisis, labor and management should coordinate. The Party and government authorities of this city have jointly issued a public announcement that both labor and management should absolutely comply with. Now, the Datong Bookstore Branch Office of the Publishing Industry Labor Union, during the preparatory period, has not been joined by all workers and has taken illegal actions, confronting the employer and forcibly announcing a strike. If this is not swiftly and severely stopped, the bookstore's business will be impaired, and the issue of local public order will be greatly affected. It is reasonable to report the situation and request your review and approval, swiftly order a cessation, and impose penalties in accordance with the law to maintain business. This is for the public good. Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, respectfully.

▲Company Notice Datong Bookstore yesterday announced to the striking workers that a portion of the employees of this bookstore illegally went on strike on the 16th of this month. On the 17th, the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs jointly issued a public notice, strictly ordering an immediate resumption of work. Fearing that the striking workers were not fully informed, this bookstore published a notice in the newspaper, extending the deadline to 12:00 noon on the 19th for a uniform resumption of work. However, in addition to a small number of people who have already extricated themselves and returned to work, the rest are still waiting and watching, coerced by malicious elements. Today, the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs have jointly issued another public notice, setting a deadline for resuming work. If they fail to resume work within three days, they will be treated as voluntary resignation, and new workers will be recruited to replenish the workforce. In order to respect the laws and decrees of the Party and government organs and to promote the awakening of the striking workers, this bookstore hereby publishes another notice, hoping that they will all go to the factory to sign in and resume work before November 21st. Otherwise, this bookstore will have no choice but to comply with the order and dismiss them in accordance with the law. This is a special announcement.

▲Labor Union Meeting A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency visited the Datong Branch Office yesterday and asked about the workers' opinions. According to them, all employees were unable to bear the pressure and were seeking to improve their treatment and conditions. The company had no sincerity in accepting their demands, leading to the strike. Currently, as the conditions have not been adequately resolved, the Party and government organs have jointly issued a public notice, setting a deadline for resuming work. However, the workers' opinion is that they will not resume work until the conditions are met. Moreover, the Labor Union has scheduled an emergency plenary meeting of the board of directors at 9:30 AM today at the Labor Union in Daqing Lane, Fusheng Road, to discuss important countermeasures. The employees will naturally await the Labor Union's orders.

▲Worker Arrested After the strike by the workers of the Datong Bookstore, the Haining Road Police Station dispatched armed plainclothes police officers to station there for the sake of local public order. At around 8:00 AM yesterday, some non-union workers prepared to enter the company to work. The striking workers believed that they were disrupting the strike discipline and tried to dissuade them. The stationed police officers intervened and detained Xu Xinong, a worker from the typesetting department, who was advising them from the side, and took him to the police station. After questioning by the police chief, he was transferred to the Special District Local Court for review.

Sanmen Bay Overseas Chinese Construction Committee

First Meeting Held in Shanghai Yesterday

The Sanmen Bay Overseas Chinese Construction Committee held its first meeting at 3:00 PM on the 18th at Xingye Co., Ltd., No. 9 Keming Lane, North Sichuan Road, Shanghai. Thirty-six members attended. The meeting was conducted as usual. Xu Xinfu was elected as the temporary chairman, and Xu Botao as the recorder. (A) The chairman reported on the progress. Last October, Chai Lianfu and Zhou Meige went to the South Seas Islands at their own expense to promote and gather overseas Chinese to return to the country and cooperate in developing Sanmen Bay. It was only today that the Construction Committee was established, after much effort. Afterwards, an inspection team was organized to conduct on-site investigations in the bay. As a result, everyone believed that development was possible. Therefore, the establishment of this committee became increasingly urgent, etc. (B) The chairman respectfully read the declaration and articles of association. (C) The number of executive and supervisory committee members was discussed, and it was decided that there would be nine executive committee members and three supervisory committee members, which was passed by a majority. (D) The executive and supervisory committee members were elected. Huang Pian, Chai Lianfu, Liu Baoyu, Xu Xinfu, Xie Shengsun, Chen Qiying, Yuan Fazhang, Wang Gechen, and Chen Zaozhen were elected as executive committee members. Liu Shimu, Xu Tingzuo, and Ye E were elected as supervisory committee members. Xu Weihui, Liu Bingsen, Jin Jixiang, Wang Benchuan, and Gui Moxin were elected as alternate executive committee members. Hu Changying was elected as an alternate supervisory committee member. (E) Liu Shimu, Chen Qiying, and Liu Baoyu were elected as review committee members to review the declaration and articles of association. (F) Temporary motion: Xu Weihui proposed that it is necessary to establish a Resettlement and Relief Committee and requested all attendees to join. Everyone agreed and joined. The registration in the Construction Committee's register was considered the standard, which was passed by everyone. Wang Zhongcui proposed that the Sanyi Highway should be started immediately and requested everyone's attention. Wang Gechen said that a Sanyi Highway Construction Committee should be organized in the future to be responsible for the handling. All highway measurement drawings and designs will be temporarily accepted and kept by this committee. Everyone agreed and passed the motion. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

Report on Southern Fujian Opium Situation from the Anti-Drug Association

This city's Chinese National Anti-Drug Association previously received reports from the Xiamen Anti-Drug Association and various organizations in Southern Fujian regarding the military's encouragement of opium seedling cultivation and the collection of taxes. This was previously reported. Now, the Association has received another telegram from the Fujian Provincial Anti-Drug General Office, stating that opium is being extensively cultivated in various counties of Fujian Province this year, mostly encouraged and taxed by the military. Opium seedlings have already been planted in Southern Fujian, as well as in Putian and Funing. Chen Zhijun, Lin Zhiren, Chen Qiyu, Hong Zhemin, and others have been approved to contract opium taxes in Zhangzhou. It is heard that the method of collecting taxes in Longxi is in the name of paying off road debts, distributed according to the number of porters usually assigned to each village. Tong'an has the highest tax amount, reportedly set at 1.2 million yuan. Chen Brigade Commander is still sending personnel to collect taxes in Jinjiang, Nan'an, Hui'an, Anxi, and other counties. He Xianzhu, the commander of the 8th District Bandit Suppression Command, has also appointed Chen Jianming, the director of the Putian Financial Reorganization Office, to concurrently collect opium seedling taxes. 30,000 mu of land have been planted in Xianyou County. More than a dozen officers have been dispatched by the Marine Corps in the five counties of Funing to encourage cultivation and distribute taxes, which is an unprecedented phenomenon in recent years. The Provincial Opium Prohibition Committee is limited in its power and cannot negotiate with the military. The provincial government still has no concrete measures. The Association urgently requests that you forward this to the National Government, urging the Fujian authorities to strictly prohibit cultivation, and also request the commanders of the Army, Navy, and Air Force to swiftly issue a strict telegram to stop the military. If they dare to protect opium cultivation, they should be executed in accordance with the law. A special investigator should be sent to Fujian to conduct an on-site investigation, which may still offer some remedy. It is heard that the Association has already forwarded the information as requested. At the same time, the Association also received telegrams from the Fuding County Chamber of Commerce, Education Association, and the Fuding All Circles Anti-Drug Movement Committee, stating that local tyrants and evil gentry in the county are relying on the power of the local military garrison to establish an Agricultural Research Institute, summoning local pests to the city for meetings and inducing farmers to cultivate opium seedlings in order to extort taxes. Unfortunately, many villagers have been seduced and are implementing cultivation. The intensity of the opium scourge is unprecedented. This phenomenon, after the central government reiterated the opium prohibition, is uniquely similar to that of Anhui Province. It is heard that the Anti-Drug Association, in view of the rampant opium cultivation, will shift most of its efforts to deal exclusively with opium cultivation incidents in Fujian and Anhui.

Various Labor Unions Telegraph the Fourth Plenary Session

To Revoke the Representative Status of Hou Dachun

The Shanghai labor unions sent a telegram to the Fourth Plenary Session in Nanjing, stating: Urgent, Nanjing Fourth Plenary Session Representatives' Assembly: Hou Dachun embezzled relief funds, and the accusers have filed a lawsuit with the court. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association and the Party Department have solemnly investigated the matter. Finally, the Shanghai Party Department submitted the case to the central government for severe punishment. Hou's suspicion of embezzlement is recognized by the public. During the central government's investigation period, Hou should be suspended from exercising all Party rights. Based on this point, on [day unclear], all Shanghai labor unions telegraphed the Credentials Committee of the Assembly, Chen, Zhou, and Ding, requesting the revocation of Hou's status as a representative to the Fourth Plenary Session. The request was not approved, causing public outrage. Today, we telegraph the Assembly again, urging you to approve and implement the request swiftly in order to uphold Party discipline and avoid disputes. We also pray for a clear response. "Northeast and Japan" Publication

The book "Northeast and Japan" was recently compiled and printed by the Northeast News Agency. The content is exceptionally rich. At a time when the Japanese invaders are rampant and taking advantage of every opportunity, our countrymen are deeply saddened and determined to study the Northeast and Japan in order to resist aggression and seek survival. This book by the News Agency aims to awaken the people of the country through the power of written propaganda. The book has nine chapters, totaling more than 100,000 words, detailing the Japanese conspiracy to invade the Northeast and the Japanese atrocities in the Northeast. It also narrates the images of the Japanese desperation and helplessness, the process of the League of Nations mediation, and the criticisms of the Japanese by various countries, all in a detailed and analytical manner. The book also includes prefaces by Chen Binhe, the president of the Japanese Research Society, and Mr. Pan Yangyao, as well as a map for easy understanding. The hardcover book is priced at sixty cents. Bulk orders are priced extremely low. In addition to being distributed by the general agent, Hongcai Bookstore, Zhiyuan Road, Zhabei, all major bookstores in this and other cities also carry the book.

Recent News from the China Machine-Made Toy Factory

The China Machine-Made Toy Factory, located in Zongyu Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei, has been operating for two years. The various colorful children's toys produced are exquisitely designed, lovely in style, brightly colored, beautiful, and the materials are more durable than imported products. The prices are also lower than imported products. Therefore, since its launch, it has been popular throughout the country. Amidst the boycott of Japanese goods, business is even more prosperous than before. With the New Year approaching, which is the peak season for toy sales, it is heard that merchants are particularly eager to order from the factory, and the factory is experiencing a large supply shortage.

Lehua Socks Factory Expands Internally

The Lehua Socks Factory on Xiaodongmen Inner Street has been operating successfully since its opening. The Green Tree brand silk thread woolen socks sold are extremely durable and affordable. As a result, buyers flock to the store. The factory director, Mr. Geng Desen, and Mr. Mei have been planning and urging the workers to actively renovate the store day and night, and the area has been expanded by more than half a丈. In the future, customers will not have to experience the same level of crowding as before.

Fuqiang Vehicle Shop Opens Today

Mr. Ye Shanxian was hired by the Tongchang Car Shop two years ago and served as the factory director of the Tongchang Vehicle Manufacturing Factory on Binlang Road. Recently, he resigned from Tongchang and organized the Fuqiang Vehicle Manufacturing Company with like-minded colleagues. The company is located opposite the Guohuo Commercial Market of the City Chamber of Commerce on North Henan Road. Preparations have been completed and business will begin today, with the official opening to be scheduled at a later date. The company specializes in bicycles, carriages, motorized bicycles, children's cars, and various vehicle parts, priced affordably.

Xiaohua Palace Restaurant Opens Today

The Xiaohua Palace Restaurant on the west side of the Great World's Yanma Road is jointly established by business tycoons Mr. Chen Rongsheng, Mr. Qiu Wanyong, Mr. Ma Juquan, and Mr. Chen Fukang. The decoration is elegant, the seating is spacious and comfortable, and famous chefs have been specially selected to prepare exquisite dishes and snacks. The restaurant also adheres to the principle of low profits to serve the community. It is scheduled to open on the 20th of this month. At that time, mountain delicacies, fine wines, and delicious dishes will surely satisfy the guests.

Shishi Daily Resurrects Tomorrow

The Shishi Daily has been suspended for half a month, and the number of letters urging its revival increases daily. Recently, the internal structure of the newspaper has been reorganized, with Dong Qimeng still serving as editor-in-chief. The content is more exciting than before, and includes new literary works by Ms. Tang Wenxuan, social novels by Mr. Wang Xiaoyi, and Lianzhu long stories, all of which are famous masterpieces. The other writers are also literary giants. It is heard that the newspaper is scheduled to be published tomorrow (the 21st).

Xiangxing Insurance Department Settles Claims Quickly

The water and fire insurance department of the Xiangxing Foreign Company at No. 2 Beijing Road in this city has a long-standing reputation. As a result, policyholders are unusually enthusiastic. This time, on October 21st, the Defulong Hardware and Grocery Store on Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei held a fire insurance policy with the company for 2,500 taels of silver. In less than five days, a fire broke out. Yu Wenjun of the water and fire insurance department personally went to investigate and confirmed the damage, and immediately paid the full amount of compensation. The procedure was quick and reliable, which is commendable.

Renhe National Goods Store Opens Today

The Renhe National Goods Store at the intersection of Xiahui Road and Songshan Road in this city was initiated by colleagues from the Renhe Midwifery School's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. The purpose is to recognize the futility of empty talk about saving the country, and to engage in practical work, collecting famous products from various provinces and forming a joint-stock company. It is scheduled to open today, with invitations extended to all sectors to visit. It is heard that the store has gifts to reward customers, which will surely be a grand occasion.

Boy Pan Jintang Missing

The boy Pan Jintang, currently 15 years old, lives in the area below the Xilou Building in Longhua. His father works as a laborer in Xujiahui. On the twelfth day of last lunar month, his mother ordered him to go to his father's place to get money. Before leaving, his mother told her son that if there was no money at his father's place, he would be beaten. When he went to his father's place, there was no money to give him, so he was afraid and did not return. He has been missing for many days. His family is very worried. If anyone knows his whereabouts, please send him to Pan Zengliang, the lithographer at the Shenbao Daily, No. 3 Ma Road, who will forward him to his parents, to reunite the family, which would be a meritorious deed. A small reward of twenty yuan will be prepared to compensate for your labor.
